                   President of the World Peace Unification Family Association, Hwang Seon-jo

1)
Our Wish
Today, I would like to speak briefly on the topic of 'Our Wish.'
When we consider the Republic of Korea, what is our wish? It is the unification of North and South Korea. Expanding the scope further, when we look at the world, our wish is to achieve a peaceful world where the democratic world and the communist world do not fight but unite as one.
This world, which has not become an ideal foundation
From an individual perspective, a person's wish would be to properly achieve what they desire in their family or workplace. However, the wishes of individuals will vary according to the various circumstances they are in. Looking at families, since they revolve around the parents, the family members' wishes will be to see the plans set by the parents come to fruition.
Thus, from individuals to the world, our wishes differ depending on our positions and circumstances. While the wishes may differ, the reality is that we all hope for them to be fully realized.
February 12, 1971 (Friday), Yeongdeungpo Church.
* This speech was given at the Yeongdeungpo District Headquarters during a night tour of nine districts in Seoul.

8   Our Wish
So, is the world we live in today truly the world I desire? Am I indeed living in an environment where I can fulfill my wishes? When we consider this, we can see that the world we live in today is not that kind of world.
We, who are born and living in this world, can always feel that we are in an environment that is contrary to the position where we can enjoy eternal happiness.
In workplaces, there are various complex issues related to the individual, and even when looking at a family, in the process of that family establishing a plan, we must ask whether we can truly consider it an ideal family foundation that we can wish for in a meaningful sense. Issues arise that indicate it is not so. Therefore, we are at a point where we must eliminate all environments that contradict our wishes surrounding our workplaces and families.
When we look at social organizations, we also feel that the organization is not a group that can eternally enjoy happiness in this society or be considered the eternal light of our wishes.
When considering the Republic of Korea itself, is it truly a country that the people wish for? In other words, does the environment established by the Republic of Korea bring happiness to each individual and enable us to achieve the peace and all the wishes we desire? When we see that such an environment is not established, we cannot view the Republic of Korea itself as a foundation for eternal happiness.
There are many advanced countries in this world. Among them, if we look at a country like the United States, the citizens living there are undoubtedly the envy of the world as citizens of the highest advanced nation. However, just because they have such an environment, can we say that the environment of that country is the eternal foundation that the citizens desire? The answer is no. There are contradictions and conflicts present there as well. This connects from the world at large down to the individual.
9 
From this perspective, whether we consider the individual, family, society, nation, or world, we find that the ideal environment we wish for is not present. When we consider whether this is truly the place we want to live forever, we cannot help but feel that this world does not meet that criterion. Therefore, today, we individuals carry a hope to seek a better place, and that is our life.
Human Wishes and the Wishes of the Absolute Being
People wish for their existence, 'I,' to do better and to succeed. They want to play a central role in their environment and, further, to become central figures in their nation. Individuals live with their own wishes to become world-renowned scholars, politicians, or saints. However, these wishes are not wishes based on their current positions; they are wishes for the future that transcend their current circumstances. They live with higher hopes for the future than they have for the present. This applies not only to individuals but also to society and nations.
The world we live in is not a destination where humanity can achieve its wishes and goals; it is a process toward achieving those ends. We must recognize that we are in a process of striving to achieve higher wishes.
Just as we humans have wishes, if there is an Absolute Being who created humanity, that Absolute Being must also have wishes. There will be wishes regarding individuals, families, nations, and the world from the perspective of the Absolute Being. For the Republic of Korea, there will be wishes regarding its citizens as the Absolute Being. When considering the authority of advanced nations centered around the United States and the missions entrusted to them in the current world, there will also be wishes regarding that. Additionally, there will be wishes regarding the democratic world.
However, should the differing wishes of individuals remain as mere personal wishes, or should they become a common wish shared by the 3 billion people of the world looking toward one place? Of course, there may be differences in relationships and hierarchies, but the direction must be the same, and we must walk the same path. If they are heading in different directions, no matter how much they may have their own wishes, they cannot establish a relationship with the ideal world, nor can they connect with the Absolute Being.
While the positions in which people find themselves differ, the desire for all humanity to reach the destination of their wishes is a common sentiment shared by everyone. When considering whether the standards of those wishes differ between people of the past, present, and future, if they do differ, true happiness cannot be attained.
If that wish is an element of absolute happiness, it must be unified across what the people of the past desired, what the present desires, and what the future will desire. That singular purpose, or the essence of the wish, is not limited to the people of Korea. It transcends nationalities and ethnicities, possessing universal validity. In other words, it must be a wish that is not focused solely on a specific ethnicity but rather serves as a common goal and a factor for collective happiness that all humanity can pursue. If it does not become that, it cannot be the happiness that humanity desires.
Then, should that wish be solely for human happiness? If there were only humans, it could be a wish solely for human happiness. However, if there is a God, or an Absolute Being, what would that Absolute Being's wish be? If the wish of the Absolute Being centers on something beyond humanity, it would have no relation to humanity. However, if the Absolute Being is related to humanity, it would not wish for a destination that is contrary to humanity's wishes.
From the perspective of Christians today, God's ideals and wishes cannot be fulfilled from a dimension that is different from humanity. Only when God's wishes and human wishes align can God's wishes be fulfilled, and the human wishes that desire the fulfillment of God's wishes can also be realized. Therefore, the fulfillment of that wish should not be hoped for solely from the perspective of the Absolute Being, but rather it should be hoped for in a place where the Absolute Being and humanity are together. This is something we cannot overlook.
The future must be better than the present, and the present must be better than the past to reach the destination.
When considering your individual conscience, your conscience wishes for the best in everything. Your conscience wants to be the best in the Republic of Korea. Furthermore, it desires to be the best in the world. Even if you are in an environment where that cannot happen, your heart still wants to be the best and desires to make the world your own. If there is something higher than this world, you do not want to stand apart from it; rather, the higher it is, the more you want to establish a relationship with it. This is an undeniable desire and heart of humanity.
When we consider students, their wish is to achieve the best grades in their school. Their desire is to achieve the best grades that surpass the historical foundation of the school from the past to the present. Based on this standard of achieving the best records, the school establishes a new historical tradition and develops.
As the standard for achieving the best grades increases, the school becomes more famous and develops. If a student who excelled ten years ago still holds the best record today, and that record has not been broken, then that school is not a developing school. In other words, if it remains in a position of recalling the past, it cannot stand in a position to advance toward new records in the future. Such a school cannot develop. However, if today is better than yesterday, and tomorrow is better than today, then that school will develop infinitely. When that school becomes such a place, it can represent all schools in the Republic of Korea. This is true for any social organization as well.
12   Our Wish
When considering families, the same applies. If a family says, "We will become the best family in the Republic of Korea. Our family, centered around love for our parents, will become a model for all families and a center for the Republic of Korea," then that family is not pursuing the past but is at the forefront of all families, welcoming the heavenly fortune that comes to the Republic of Korea. Do you understand?
When considering the Republic of Korea, whether it thrives or declines depends on whether it can raise the standards of value step by step, focusing on more valuable content than the past and present. Therefore, if the Republic of Korea gradually raises its standards, it can remain, but if the present does not surpass the standards of the past, we must understand that it will regress.
Furthermore, when considering the democratic world and the communist world, there may have been times when either was at its peak, but that time is not the peak; it is a time of vigorous progress toward the peak. When that process raises its standards from the past to the present and from the present to the future, that world can approach a more valuable destination of wishes. However, if the present is worse than the past, that world will move further away from the valuable destination of wishes.
To develop oneself
Until today, the United States has provided economic aid to underdeveloped countries from a leading position representing democracy. When the United States struggles to overcome the suffering of underdeveloped countries while taking responsibility for all policy influences centered around the world, all countries come to have trust in the United States. And all countries can rise by using the United States as a springboard. However, if that does not happen, the gap between the United States and other countries will inevitably widen. The leading position of the United States in the democratic world must not face a path of retreat.
The same applies to the communist world. If the Soviet Union, which leads the communist world, stands in a position that only thinks about and longs for the past rather than the present, it is already on a path of regression.
The same is true for individual desires. People want to possess the most precious things in the world. That is human desire. So, what is the most precious thing in this world? From the perspective of a world without the Absolute Being, what could be the most precious thing? Is it money? When comparing material and people, people are more precious than material. Among people, who is the most precious? One cannot help but think of oneself as the most precious. Therefore, among people, one’s own self is the most precious.
Everyone thinks that they are the most precious. Even elderly people who are nearing the end of their lives believe that they are the most precious. This is the same for young children and youth. Adults feel the same way. People do not like to be in environments where they feel infringed upon or intimidated by others.
Relationships are established around oneself, and one wishes to influence others through oneself. This desire extends beyond families to society, nations, and the world.
People want to be a central figure based on themselves. However, is the existence of 'I' truly a central existence in the Republic of Korea? It is uncertain, but regardless, everyone wishes to be the center and hopes that it will be so.
Then, are the positions of the 30 million citizens of the Republic of Korea all the same? No, they are not. There are those who are behind and those who are ahead, those who are high and those who are low; everyone is in a different position. If someone wishes to establish a relationship with something that is higher and more valuable than anything else, they cannot remain passive. In other words, simply sitting and shouting, "Oh! The Republic of Korea is mine!" will not make it so.
If one wishes to enter a position where such relationships can be established, they must overcome trials proportional to that wish. They must go through that difficult process to develop a subjectivity that possesses universal validity. If one wishes for their desires to be fulfilled without going through that, confusion will ensue.
Therefore, there is a constitution that presents the requirements and directions of principled guidance centered around the nation, guiding the people by providing all the guidelines for the people's lives. If one violates that law, they cannot proceed. Without law, one cannot reach the desired place, so in trying to align the direction with the law to reach the desired place, although the positions of thirty million citizens are different, they must all be governed by the same law and cannot deviate from it.

To reach a certain position, one must overcome the corresponding difficulties. When considering whether you can affirm that tomorrow will be better than today in reality, if the standard becomes one that the nation expects, then you can take responsibility for the nation. Furthermore, when it manifests with values that exceed the world, people will automatically follow your guidance, whether they want to or not.

What do people wish to become? They aspire to be great figures or saints. They want to become significant individuals. However, to become a great person, one cannot remain idle. One must overcome the difficulties that correspond to that greatness.

When looking at the nation, for any country to reach the standards of a developed nation, its citizens cannot remain idle. They must overcome numerous difficulties. Citizens of any country must pave the way for victories that correspond to the challenges that others have not overcome. Only when the value is gradually solidified and the results prominently appear before various nations can the citizens of that country claim the authority or position of a developed nation.

From this perspective, if there is an absolute being, the desire that the absolute being has for humanity cannot escape the relationship with humans. In other words, if the ancestors of humanity lived together with the absolute being from the very beginning, then the absolute being and the ancestors of humanity would have been completely aligned from that time. In such a position, the desire that the absolute being has for the ancestors of humanity is merely individual, but the desire of that individual is undoubtedly a global and cosmic desire.

You are individual beings, but your individual desires are cosmic. Everything in the world aligns with your desires. If there is a cosmic master, there must be a relative existence that can serve that master, and to do so, one must become a being that can match the disposition of the cosmic master. Yet, despite this, can one have a petty and trivial mindset? That would lead to nothing.

When we focus on our ancestors, it is certain that they would want to possess the entire world just as we think. If our ancestors had been able to interact completely with the absolute being and act in a way that fulfills the desires of that absolute being, what would humanity be like today? If that were the case, the desires of humanity would have begun to be fulfilled from that time.

If humanity had become one with God, what position would God want to establish in relation to humanity? God's intention in relating to humans is not merely to make humans happy; rather, it is to achieve happiness for God as well through the happiness of humans.

So, when we consider the relationship between God and humanity, what position does humanity hold before God? In other words, is it the position of a servant, a child, or an adopted child? If God loves humanity, what position would God want to treat humanity from? If we view it from the perspective of human desires, being treated as a servant would be undesirable, and being treated as an adopted child would also be undesirable. If there is a position that humanity can absolutely hope for before God, it would be the position where one can say, "You are my Father, and I am Your child." For women, it would be, "You are my Father, and I am Your daughter." There is no higher position for humanity than this.

If there were an opportunity to become the son or son-in-law of the President of the Republic of Korea, and one were asked, "Would you like to be the President's son or son-in-law?" everyone would choose to be the son of the sovereign, right? Similarly, if there were a world president, the extent to which one can emotionally connect with that president who leads the world would determine how much one can rise to a position of glory.

From this perspective, if there is an absolute God in this universe, what kind of relationship would God and humanity want to establish? They desire to aspire to a single position. Not the position of a servant, nor that of an adopted child, but the position of sons and daughters. This is the desire of humanity, isn't it? In other words, if there is a highest desire that humanity can hope for from the absolute God, it is to rise to the position of being the sons and daughters of the absolute being.

Then, what should one do after becoming the sons and daughters of God? Should one be disobedient to their parents and be in a position that does not please their parents, receiving their reproach? That cannot be. One must fulfill the duty of filial piety to their parents, becoming children who make their parents so happy that they cannot help but love them. That is all that humanity desires.

Therefore, humanity must become the sons and daughters who receive God's love. If the ancestors of humanity became the beloved sons and daughters of God, a blood relationship that cannot be severed would have been established between God, the parent, and humanity, the children. When one becomes a child who can receive the love of their parent, what belongs to the parent becomes the child’s. For example, even if the house one lives in was built by their parents, they can still say, "This is my house." A kindergarten child born in that house, who has never seen their parents build it, can still grow up saying, "This house is ours, this house is mine." Would the parents feel bad when they hear that? Rather, they would find it endearing when their child says, "This is my house." Because it is both the father's house and the child's house, it is not an exaggeration to say that. Humanity recognizes this.

Similarly, even if humans have not seen the absolute being who created the universe, or do not know that relationship, if they are called children of God, then the universe belongs to God, and whose is it? It belongs to the children of God, doesn't it? So, if the children of God say, "This universe is mine," would the Father feel bad? If a child says they can manage better than the Father, would the Father say, "Hey, you little brat, how dare you!"? Parents do not react that way.

When Joseph told his brothers, "In my dream, the sun, the moon, and eleven stars bowed down to me," his brothers were jealous because they thought his words were arrogant, but their father and mother did not feel bad. They simply said, "Let's see where this goes." This reflects the heart of a parent.

If God became the parent of humanity and humanity became the sons and daughters of God, then who does the created world, which God governs, belong to? It belongs to both God and humanity. It becomes ours. If that were the case, how immense would the value of humanity be? Would humanity envy God? There is no need to envy God. God is in my heart, in my body, and in my life. There is no need to even think about whether God exists or not.

If that were the case, God would not be an abstract concept to be pursued; rather, God would be a being that can be felt in life and aligned with in life. Therefore, humanity does not need to strive to dominate the world. What would one do by making the world theirs? If one can make God theirs, then the world becomes theirs. Do you think that is possible or not?

If humanity were in such a position, the desires you pursue now, the workings of your heart, would be unnecessary. Originally, you should not have been in the position you are in now; rather, you should have started from possessing God and, from that foundation, moved forward. Then, the place where you were born would not have been an unhappy place but a happy one.

Those with parents are not pitiful. Children who can receive eternal love from their parents and live in a free environment without even facing small trials are happy people. What if humanity had started with such an environment from the beginning? The thoughts of seeking success or making the world theirs would have been unnecessary; everything would have been achieved. Without even thinking about establishing a relationship with something higher than the world, relationships would have already been established.

Broken Humanity

However, humanity has lost everything because it could not start from such a position. We are well aware that throughout history, countless prophets and sages have died while pursuing a better and more valuable world, continuing along the path of struggle. Yet, the time they hoped for has not yet been realized. Therefore, you have the heart to strive for something more valuable, a more brilliant path in life, and a more meaningful world.

The ultimate purpose of humanity is not to conquer the world but to conquer God. It does not end with conquering God; it aims to reach a position where one can receive God's love. Therefore, what is humanity's highest desire? It is for those who have not reached such a position to stand in that position. Standing in such a position is humanity's highest desire.

Then, what is God's desire for humanity, who loves humanity? It is to save humanity from this world of Satan. God does not delight in seeing humanity suffering and in pain in the world of hell. God wants to establish a loving relationship with all people and live together with them. From the perspective of such a Father, saving us is God's desire. Therefore, God's desire aligns with humanity's desire. The alignment of desires signifies a relationship of love. Do you understand?

When we look at ourselves quietly, the problem is that our body and mind are not united and are always in conflict, right? Within my singular entity, my body and mind pursue two different purposes. If God had created humanity to go towards two purposes, then God would not be absolute. If God created humanity with a single thought and a single purpose, then humanity cannot be born as a being with two purposes.

Yet, considering the fact that humanity is in such a contradictory situation, it indicates that humanity did not start normally in a good sense. It suggests that we are in a broken position, or that the absence of God has led to such results from the very beginning. One of these two is the problem. However, if God exists and such results have come about, it indicates that humanity has gone wrong. Humanity is broken. Therefore, the brokenness must be repaired.

That is why God has been working to establish a repair factory to fix the brokenness throughout history. That is what religion is. If a repair factory is established, there must be a technician, and that technician is the leaders of religion.

Today, humanity is like a broken radio. Therefore, we must be repaired to become normal people. To do this, one must enter the repair factory. One must go through the repair factory. Looking at history, we see that the world's cultural realms have been absorbed into the realm of religious culture. Whether it is the Christian cultural realm centered around the democratic world, the cultural realm of Confucianism, Buddhism, and Taoism centered in East Asia, the Hindu cultural realm centered in India, or the Islamic cultural realm, we can see that for thousands of years, people have flocked into the realm of religious culture. This is similar to how all the necessary components gather around a repair factory once it is established. When we observe these facts, you must understand that God is working.

The ultimate point of desire that you are currently hoping for, the final desire that humanity can aspire to, is to exist in the same position as God. In other words, God's desire must be humanity's desire, and humanity's desire must be God's desire. What belongs to God must belong to me, and what belongs to me must belong to God. God's love must be my love, and my love must be God's love. This is the position we aspire to. When such a relationship can be established, humanity will have no further desires. However, as mentioned earlier, humanity is already sick, like a broken radio.

The Completion of Humanity is God's Desire

If humanity had become the sons and daughters who could receive God's eternal love, that is, if the ancestors of humanity had started from a position of complete oneness with God, that beginning could have been both an individual beginning and the beginning of a cosmic existence. Furthermore, if humanity had not fallen and had grown as the beloved sons and daughters of God, fully receiving God's unique love, then humanity would have nothing more to desire. That would be the end. Being in that position means being an individual, yet a cosmic individual.

If all things created belong to the absolute being, then humanity, as the children of that being, also belongs to that being. Therefore, if humanity had stood in that position, it would have achieved individual completion while simultaneously fulfilling God's purpose of creation. Right? The completion of God's sons and daughters is also the completion of all things created by God. If everything is completed in this way, what would God be like? Would God feel bad seeing humanity completed? God would rejoice.

If an artist has devoted much effort to completing a work, that artist would want to cherish that work and leave it for future generations. They would want to preserve that work forever. How much more would God, if humanity were in a position to receive God's love as beloved sons and daughters, not just love humanity for a few months or years and then cast them aside? If humanity lives for about a hundred years, would God love them for a hundred years and then say, "I no longer need you," and throw them away? No. Just as humanity desires to leave behind the work they have painstakingly completed for their descendants, wanting to keep it with them, how much more would God want to do the same? God would want to love humanity, born as beloved sons and daughters, forever.
Yes. Because the absolute being must be in a position to be that joyful, humans must also attain eternal life. Wouldn't that be so? It means that we cannot remain forever in a transient state. 

If Adam and Eve, the ancestors of humanity, had achieved this, then the completion of Adam and Eve would naturally mean the fulfillment of all of God's desires. Isn't that right? The completion of Adam and Eve signifies that all of God's wishes regarding humans, who are the center of all creation, would be fulfilled. If that had happened, how joyful would God have been? If we are the sons and daughters of such a joyful Father, what should we do? We must be joyful. To what extent should we be joyful? Should it be more than the joy of a father and son reuniting after decades of separation during the Korean War, embracing each other and shedding tears of joy, or less? There is no need for comparison. It is the highest joy. No one but God can occupy that joy. Therefore, should we have misfortune, or should we have happiness? Of course, we should have happiness.

The completion of the couple becomes the starting point for the completion of the family. In other words, the completion of the family is the completion of the children and the couple. Isn't that so? If parents are living happily in God's love, would the children born to those parents go to a place of suffering and crying? They would not. Therefore, what is the completion of the couple? "It is the completion of the family." According to the principles of the Unification Church, it is the completion of the son-in-law expectation.

From such a completed family, another completed family emerges. When that happens, those families will form tribes, leading to tribal completion, then national completion, and further to world completion. That position is not where you wish to be number one in the world, but rather a position that you all must fully realize and digest.

Why do humans desire the number one position in the world? It is because humans are broken. There is no time to discuss this in detail, but you are broken. The world we live in today is not the world we desire. Even looking at the Republic of Korea, it is not the nation we wish for. The same goes for society. There are many conditions here that we need to correct and resolve. Therefore, this society is not the ideal society we desire.

Originally, if the human ancestors had united centered on the absolute God, then from there, the completion of the couple, family, nation, and world would have been achieved. Not only the completion of the world but also the completion of the universe would have been realized. Since we have lost such things, the original heart of humanity yearns for them, doesn’t it?

A broken radio does not function properly, but when it receives a signal, it still makes a sound, even if it is just a beep. Similarly, humans have a true heart that, through its action, seeks to go somewhere. That place is the highest place. You feel the same way, don’t you? Surely you do.

So, humans are broken. We are broken beings. What good does it do for a broken human to boast about their abilities? We need to disassemble and fix ourselves again. When a broken machine enters a repair shop, what happens? Do they just leave it as it is? What do they do? They repair it, right? To repair it, everything must be disassembled. You might feel uncomfortable thinking about it, but your situation is just like that.

Thus, what is religion? It is a repair shop for broken humans. However, when this repair shop ends, it should not just be a matter of replacing parts. Therefore, the Unification Church aims to create a comprehensive repair shop that conducts repairs in a holistic manner. There cannot just be a comprehensive repair shop; there must be technicians for the comprehensive repair shop. Who is this technician? It is the Lord of the Second Advent, as spoken of in Christianity. From this perspective, the time has come for all religions in the world to come to an end, and if the Unification Church has emerged as a comprehensive repair shop, then all people desiring a unified religion should welcome us. Moreover, we should take pride as the Korean people that the Unification Church has arisen in Korea, more than any other country in the world. Even if the Unification Church fails to fulfill such a mission, if it at least points in that direction, this nation should appreciate and welcome it. Nevertheless, the Unification Church is currently facing opposition. Isn’t that so? "Yes, we are facing opposition."

Why is that? When a repair shop repairs a broken machine, it must fix what is broken, but until now, the repair shops have not even known what was broken and have made things worse. The owner of such a repair shop should perish. Since they have caused their own downfall, they oppose us to avoid destruction. They oppose us as a nation and even as a world. However, even if the nation and the world all oppose us, our repair shop will never perish.

Humans that need to be repaired

A broken radio or television can be fixed by someone who knows where it is broken, and it only needs to be repaired once. Then, just like a new radio or television, everyone can listen to and watch the broadcasts sent from the station. It doesn’t matter if there are a hundred or a thousand; they are all the same. Even if there are billions, it is the same. Likewise, when God enters the hearts of humans and they become joyful, if there were a television that reflects that joy, then everyone could feel that joyful heart. Would your hearts be joyful or not? It would produce sounds of joy. And when God is sad, it would produce sounds of sadness. If all people became like that, how wonderful would this world be? But since it is not like that, you need to be repaired.

So, do you want to enter the repair shop and be repaired slowly, or do you want to be repaired quickly? That depends on each of your hearts. Some may be repaired in a year, while others may take ten years, and some may enter the repair shop and be left there for a lifetime without being repaired.

If the human progenitors had become one with God, there would be no such problems. That would be individual completion and world completion, the joy of the individual and the joy of the world. If that had happened, it would have been heaven all at once. However, since this was not achieved, it must be achieved again. When that happens, the family, tribe, nation, and world will naturally be completed. If the family is completed, everything will naturally fall into place.

If God planted the true pine seed, then a true pine sprout would emerge. It would remain a true pine forever. Isn’t that so? However, humans have not been able to do that. They should have become true pine seeds, but they became something else. Therefore, they must return to being true pine seeds. So, metaphorically speaking, they have become wild olive trees.

Today, humans have become wild olive trees. Originally, they should have become true olive trees, but they have become wild olive trees. The fruit of such a tree is only fit for crows.

So, how can one become a true olive tree? They must be grafted. The wild olive tree must be cut off and grafted onto the true olive tree. Therefore, today, we humans must also enter the regeneration process and engage in the grafting process. Do you understand?

From the perspective of humans who have not become true olive trees, it can be said that humans have lost the ideal world. They have lost the ideal nation. The Republic of Korea is not an ideal nation. It is a nation where evil prevails. This world is also a world where evil prevails. It is in a position where good and evil are mixed together. This situation must be dissected and cut away. If good and evil are in conflict with each other, it is impossible to establish an ideal nation or world.

The history waiting for the marriage of true sons and daughters

That is why the Unification Church aims to establish a heavenly kingdom on earth. Without establishing a heavenly kingdom on earth, one cannot enter the heavenly kingdom in heaven.
The Unification Church is a progressive, proactive, and inclusive religion. When I say this, people in the world will say, “The Unification Church members are good at propaganda.” So what if I do some propaganda? (Laughter) Now it is time to promote. The people of the world are equipped to act in a way that they can die at my command, transcending borders, so it is time to promote. Isn’t that right? Such feats are things that the President of the Republic of Korea or the President of the United States cannot do. Even the Prime Minister of the United Kingdom cannot do it. What I am doing now is something that Jesus and Confucius could not do. So, isn’t it worth bragging? I should try to boast about it. If you take this the wrong way, you will feel pain and distress. Such things are happening. Therefore, you must understand this clearly.
To fulfill our wish, we must walk this path. So, should you die for your country or not? “You should die.” Should the country sacrifice for the world or not? “It should sacrifice.” That is why if the United States stands in a position of democracy only for itself, it will inevitably perish. It must stand in a position to sacrifice its nation for the world. All matters must be handled from there.
Whether it is communism in China or the Soviet Union, they try to dominate the world centered on China or the Soviet Union, but where is the principle in that? If one cannot come out with a philosophy that transcends the nation and the tribe, they cannot unify the world. If one cannot transcend their own nation, they will perish.
Our wish is to serve God from the position of governing the universe. If God exists, would He want to make only the American people the masters of the world? Wouldn’t He want to make all people in the world the masters?
Will it be? Isn't that right? That's why all ideologies centered around the nation flow away. Do you understand? No matter how powerful an ideology may be to shake the world, if it cannot transcend its own ethnicity, it will ultimately perish. 

Therefore, the Unification Church argues that we must transcend our ethnicity. Although we live within the limited environment of the Republic of Korea, we should live from a perspective that transcends the nation for the world. The young women of Korea may have black hair, but the young women of the Unification Church would agree to marry yellow Western men. It is said that such a time must come to form the world as one. For women, it is sufficient if the man is Western; what more could be lacking?

Even now, about 300 Japanese people are undergoing training, but the most important thing is where they love more. Do they love the world more, or do they love their own ethnicity more? When one focuses on their own country, they perish together with it when the nation falls. This is a principle. Therefore, in order to pursue something greater, I, who am in a smaller position, must sacrifice myself; otherwise, there is no way forward.

Saints have died while proclaiming worldism, but because they lived with that ideology on earth, when the time of liberation comes on earth, the time of liberation will also occur in the spirit world, allowing them to finally meet their time and go to a place of glory. Jesus, while on the cross, prayed for the blessings of his enemies, and although he died, he maintained his integrity and walked the path of death with dignity, right? He died solely for the sake of heaven and earth, despite the opposition of the Israelite people. If he died like that, until such a world comes, we serve him as the center. The principle of heaven is to want to serve and live with that person as the master. Thus, humans are taught to "do good." Here, being good means to sacrifice. Do you understand?

Those who silently sacrifice for the nation leave descendants who can receive the fortune of the nation, and those who silently sacrifice for the world leave descendants who can receive the fortune of the world. 

Therefore, where should the Unification Church go? Today, we live in the limited environment of the Republic of Korea, but we are not nationalists. We are worldists with a greater ideology. Do you understand? That is why we have faced persecution from the Free Party, the Democratic Party, and the current regime in the Republic of Korea. Why? Because we see that the ideology is great. Thus, we are also being persecuted by both the democratic world and the communist world. We have come this far. We are not only worldists but also cosmicists. Do you understand?

Then, for what should this world sacrifice? For God…. Then, for what should God sacrifice? He must sacrifice for His love. Faith, hope, and love—these three will always exist, but which is the greatest? "It is love." The conclusion has already been reached that love is the greatest. God is also love, so He cannot live without love.

God has lost His beloved sons and daughters, so He has come out to find children whom He can love. Yes, the world must sacrifice for God, and for whom must God sacrifice? He must sacrifice for His sons and daughters. Then, what does God want to do when He meets His sons and daughters? To leave behind the one and only bond of love…. Without leaving that behind, a successor cannot emerge. From there, all relationships will finally unfold horizontally.

Therefore, we ourselves must resemble God. Without resembling God, we cannot lead this world and go before Him. In other words, we must stand in a position where we can be one with God for our wishes to be fulfilled. That is why, as I mentioned earlier, the ideology of a family that can represent humanity centered on the bond of true parents becomes the ideology of a tribe. Moreover, such a tribal ideology develops into a national ideology, and the national ideology develops into a global ideology, and also, the national ideology develops into a global ideology. Thus, the global ideology unfolds and develops into God's ideology in all aspects of life.

In this way, the desire of all created beings is to exist in a position where they can govern the entire universe centered on God's love, and you must clearly understand that this is the desire of humanity.

February 13, 1971 (Saturday), Yongsan Church.
* This message was given during the night tour of the nine districts of Seoul at the Yongsan district headquarters.

Please look down upon Your children gathered here today. This is the Yongsan district headquarters. A small group has bowed before You. They have gathered not to follow anyone else but to follow You, and they have gathered to prepare themselves as Your children, so please be present with us here. Please look into our hearts and remove all hearts that are unworthy before You, and we earnestly hope and wish that we can deny ourselves and become beings that can align with Your heart.

We must not only call You Father with words and concepts but must become sons and daughters who can serve You through our lives. If there are sons and daughters who cannot do this, please hold them and guide them so that they can come to that position. Command us before the new purpose, and we earnestly hope and wish that we may live within Your grace and be allowed to live because of You.

Father, we thank You for allowing us to meet again today in this place where we have not been able to come for a long time. Please have compassion on all the efforts of Your son who is responsible for the Yongsan district. Please have compassion on the fact that he is struggling to fulfill the important responsibility of establishing the entire Yongsan district before Your will through this small place.

It is not a matter of whether there are many people, but whether there is even one true son or daughter whose heart can resonate with Yours, whose body can connect with Yours, and who can respond before Your will, Your life, and Your heart. We know that the issue is whether even one life can appear to connect with heaven in this small place and to connect with us, so that we can become filial sons and daughters who can make You rejoice, and that You may establish us as sons and daughters who are worthy of Your pride and praise.

In the year 1971, we must have a heart of fear that we might leave conditions of resentment before the nation if we do not fulfill the mission and responsibility You have entrusted to us. As we feel that we are in a position where we can be slandered before the thirty million people of our nation, we earnestly hope and wish that we may fulfill the responsibilities entrusted to us this year and become sons and daughters who can be praised before You, who can be worthy of Your pride.

Please be present with us here, and connect our circumstances completely with Your circumstances, so that our wishes may become one with Your wishes and that Your will may be fulfilled here. Thus, may the holy foundation of victory that You love and can remain in be expanded and developed through this small group of people who have knelt down. We earnestly wish that You may be present with the children who always gather their hearts to pray for this place.

Asking You to be present with us during this one hour You have permitted, I pray all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen.

<Words> Our Unification Church does not have a long history, but we know that we have gone through a difficult history like a cloud until now. 

Looking at God's providential history since the fall of humanity, the Old Testament era was the era of offering all things as sacrifices, and the New Testament era was the era of sending a beloved son to stand in a sacrificial position, and we know that Christianity, centered on the New Testament, has developed up to now due to the merit of the sacrifice of that son who died on the cross. We know that the current era is not the era of children but the era in which parents must walk the historical path of suffering.

The history of humanity is a providential history that seeks to find a true man.
God's providential history is a history of re-creation, so in order to find what has been lost, we must follow the same order as when it was created. God created humanity after creating all things. The human ancestors, Adam and Eve, fell from their position as children before becoming true husband and wife. If these children had not fallen and had grown to stand in the position of true parents, receiving God's inheritance, this world would indeed have become a world of goodness and hope, our homeland. However, because Adam and Eve fell, they could not have the original bond of parents that God intended to establish. Although they had the bond of children, we know that Adam and Eve could not stand as children whom God could love unconditionally, placing all His hopes upon them.

Furthermore, all things should have been governed by the perfected children, Adam and Eve, but we also know that they were not governed. Therefore, the history of restoration and salvation is a history of finding the lost bond of all things, children, and parents. Thus, in the Old Testament era, it centered on all things, and in the New Testament era, it centered on children. Then, in the era of the completed testament, a new historical era centered on parents unfolds, which we members of the Unification Church understand.

When we look at the historical process that has unfolded, the history of humanity has sought to establish a center and from that center establish a family, and from that family develop into a tribe, a nation, and a world. This is the providence of God centered on religion.

So, what has religion done until now? Until now, religion has been working to find the lost Adam and Eve. In finding Adam and Eve, since God created Adam first, we must first find and establish Adam. Thus, religion has been working to find a man who can appear as a son qualified to receive God's love and can be accepted.

That is why, if you look at any religion, the founders are all men. Because the standard of the completed man in God's ideal world of creation has not been established, religion has been repeatedly seeking to find, establish, and create a new completed man among humanity, which is in a state of death.

Therefore, the content and principles of salvation that religion has pursued until now have been individual salvation. Religion has always advocated individual salvation and has worked to save individuals. When one man is perfected, a woman can be found through that man. When God created humanity, He created Adam and then created Eve based on Adam. This is the principle of creation, so unless a completed man appears, a completed woman cannot be found. Thus, we must understand that the history up to now has been one of seeking a completed man.

The history of Christianity centered on Jesus.
So God sent one person to this earth who would inherit God's love and serve as a central figure representing all humanity or all men. That person is Jesus Christ, who came and went about 2,000 years ago. When Jesus Christ came to this earth, if he had received God's love and the love of the Israelite nation and Judaism of that time, that is, if God loved him from above and the Israelite nation honored him from below, then God's love could have been connected to that nation centered on Jesus. However, because the Israelite nation could not honor Jesus, the Jesus Christ whom God sent as the perfected man could not establish a victorious foundation with the nation or the church on this earth, and thus he went to the cross. Because Jesus went to the cross, God has been working through Christianity to establish a new nation and a new state, and to find and establish a new man on this earth. The history of Christianity until now has been about expanding the foundation where that man can be honored by a woman.

If at the time Jesus came, Judaism and the nation of Israel had provided an environment where a perfected woman could meet him, then Jesus, as a perfected man, would have welcomed a perfected woman and would have established a new family that God desired to create centered on humanity at the time of creation. If that had happened, we would have seen the beginning of a perfect family at that time. The purpose of God creating man and woman was for Adam and Eve to perfect their union as husband and wife, so these two men and women should have seen the beginning of a perfect family, but that did not happen. Because Jesus came to this earth as a perfected man, if he had welcomed a perfected woman amidst the nation and the church, the beginning of a perfected family would have been established, and from that perfected family, a perfected church, a perfected nation, and a perfected world would have been formed. This was God's will.

However, because this will was not fulfilled and Jesus went to the cross, the history of Christianity in the New Testament era has been about expanding the scope to fulfill that will on a global scale. What has Christianity done until now? It has expanded outwardly the framework of a single nation like Israel. While it has expanded that framework centered on one nation, it has also expanded it globally to form the current democratic world. Thus, Christianity has taken on the ideological responsibility within this democratic world.

Christianity and the democratic world must establish a church and a nation that can provide a foundation for the perfected son of God to establish a perfected family. If at the time of Jesus, a perfected woman had been established among the Jewish church and the nation of Israel, uniting with Jesus to form the ideal family that God desired, then from that family, a tribe that could please God would have emerged, a nation would have emerged, and the world would have emerged. However, because that hope was not fulfilled, the history of Christianity is about finding that again. Therefore, Christianity has a mission to unfold a new history. This is what we call the thought of the Second Coming.

Second Coming Ideals
So, how will the Lord who is to come again appear? He will come to this earth as a true son who has the qualifications to surpass all the evils of the world, representing men in the course of human history, and to please God. What will he do when he comes to this earth? It is not to govern the nation or move the world immediately. While that may be an indirect purpose, the most direct purpose he must fulfill first is to establish a perfected woman with a perfected man. That is, a man and a woman who have completely escaped the ties of the fall must form a marital bond and establish a family. Because the ancestors of humanity failed to establish the true marital bond centered on God due to the fall, they have gone through 6,000 years of history to achieve this. Therefore, the one who comes again to establish a new marital bond and to see the beginning of a new family centered on God is the Lord of the Second Coming, and you must understand that this is the ideal of the Second Coming.

Through the true marital bond, we must develop into true children, true tribes, true nations, and a true world. However, even if such a central family is established, the surroundings of that family are not all heavenly families but are surrounded by evil families that oppose heaven. We must bring all these evil families into alignment with the will and integrate them with heaven. From one family, we must form numerous families, from those families, a new tribe, from that tribe, a new nation. The leaders of that nation should not be just any human but must be sons and daughters whom God loves, centered on heaven. Such a new nation must emerge on this earth.

In this world, there are many countries, but when we look at the sovereigns of those countries, they are not the sovereigns who inherit the responsibilities that God has desired through thousands of years of history. They are sovereigns who have been elected by their societies based on some public achievement that represents their nation or have taken such positions themselves. They are not the sovereigns who have the foundation of a central couple equipped to inherit God's love and all of God's ideals. This is an undeniable fact. There are many countries on this earth, but there are no such countries.

If there had been no fall on this earth, the whole world would have been governed and ruled by the beloved sons of God. However, since the fall, we have been governed by the evil sovereigns within the realm of evil. In light of this fact, this world is not the kingdom of heaven but a world under the dominion of evil Satan, outside of heaven and outside of God's will. Since God cannot fulfill His will centered on such a world, you must understand that He is conducting a restoration history or salvation history to return this world to a new world.

The Mission of Current Unification Members
Before a true nation can emerge to restore the world, a family centered on God must come forth that can fulfill the ideal of a son and daughter whom God loves. Then, centered on this true family, a true tribe must emerge, and centered on that true tribe, a true nation must emerge.

In this evil world, there are many nations, but among those nations, one nation that God can love must emerge and absorb the nations of the evil world. A good nation centered on God must go through the struggle of good and evil, absorbing all the evil nations, so that all the nations of the world can unite into a nation that God can directly govern, centered on God. You must understand this.

From this perspective, what is the mission that current Unification members bear? When we examine the path and mission that Unification members must take, it is not simply to gather and interact centered on the Unification Church. Believing in the Unification Church is not the path that Unification members must take. Unification members must unite centered on this organization and absorb all of humanity into the realm of unification thought beyond the nation. Thus, this must become the foundation that God can love, creating a world where many nations can converge. Without doing this, you must understand that a unified world cannot be achieved.

So, what must the Unification Church do? It must unify all churches. Christianity must not remain as it is. If there is a true tribe, it must serve as a model to restore many false tribes to true tribes. If there is a true nation, it must engraft false nations onto the true nation. If there is a true country, it must engraft false countries onto the true country.

What is the mission we must fulfill today? Here in the Yongsan district, it is not just the gathering of dozens of members in this small room that is the path for our Unification Church members. Even though a small group is gathered in this little room, they must understand that the destination they must envision is a path toward the will beyond the world.

To walk that path, you must first unify your individual selves. To do this, you must remove evil and leave only goodness. It is not about unifying centered on evil but unifying centered on goodness, so you must prioritize goodness and eliminate evil. You must focus on what is good, repel what is evil, and allow goodness to occupy the foundation of evil. Without doing so, you cannot see a unified self.

Due to the fall of our human ancestors, humanity has been placed in a position between good and evil. Therefore, one can become a good person or an evil person. By taking one step to the right, one can become a good person; by taking one step to the left, one can become an evil person. You must understand that we are individuals who are governed by these two opposing masters and their opposing purposes.

When it comes to my existence, I cannot even freely do as I wish centered on myself. Even if I resolve to do something for a year, I often find myself doing more of what I do not want than what I desire in my daily life. So, when I look back on the year, I often feel regret about the things I did during that time.

Why is that? The reason I do not go where I want and instead go where I do not want is that there is a stronger force pulling me in the direction I do not want than the force that pulls me toward what I desire. You must understand this. In other words, the individual self is placed in the middle of good and evil. It stands at the center of good and evil. Therefore, my individual self is subject to both the dominion of good and the dominion of evil. You must recognize that these two lines of division are connected to your individual self.

What you must think about here is that because the absolute God created humanity, humans must aim for a single, perfect purpose. The absolute purpose of God cannot be twofold. If the absolute God created all things, then all things were created with the plan to harmonize around the purpose of the great universe. Therefore, the purpose of existence cannot be twofold; it must be one.

However, when we look at our individual selves, we realize that we live with two purposes. There is the purpose that the heart desires, and there is the purpose that the body desires. The body and heart do not align; they always fight against each other. They are mixed up in conflict, both front and back, left and right. This is the struggle we face throughout our lives. This has been true not only for ourselves but also for the many ancestors who have come before us. It will be the same for our descendants in the future. Therefore, we must put an end to this struggle and stand in a position where we can follow only the good that the heart desires and eliminate the evil that the heart does not want.

If we do not block the path toward the purpose of evil and do not walk the one-way path toward the purpose of good, we cannot determine that our individual selves stand in a position of goodness. If we cannot make that determination, we are in a position where we hold onto both good and evil, not just good. Therefore, humanity has been fighting to cut off one of these two. That is, the heart and body are in conflict. The heart urges the body to act in goodness. It calls for helping the needy and emphasizes the need to sacrifice for others, even if it is difficult for oneself. However, we know that the body takes the opposite direction.

In this context, what current Unification members absolutely must do is to conquer the body completely with the heart within themselves, establishing the foundation for the victory of the body. Only then can we leave behind a day, a year, ten years, or a lifetime of living focused on goodness. We must become an unchanging 'I' that can focus solely on goodness. Becoming such an 'I' is of utmost importance.

Democracy and Communism as the Fruits of the History of Good and Evil
Both good and evil undoubtedly pursue global desires. The desire of a good conscience also pursues global desires, and the desire for evil also pursues global desires. Therefore, when we look at our own desires, we see that even though we do not stand in a perfect position of goodness, our wishes are global wishes. The desire to be the best in the world or to make the world ours is a desire that both the heart and body possess.

Since this is the fundamental nature of humanity, God must inevitably carry out a history that separates those who prioritize the heart from those who prioritize the body. Even if it is not taught individually, such a history must be carried out collectively. If there is an organization that prioritizes evil externally, then internally, a new organization that prioritizes good must be separated. If there is a nation centered on evil externally, then internally, a nation centered on good must be separated. If there is an evil world, then a good world must be separated internally. This separation does not happen without conflict. Just as your body and heart are in conflict, there must be a process of struggle to achieve this separation.

However, it must not remain as two indefinitely. At some point, it must be separated and ultimately resolved. Good and evil cannot coexist. Good and evil cannot exist together, and what must remain here is not evil but good. Therefore, a global end must come where evil can be completely eliminated centered on good.

In Christianity, it is said that the end will come. So, when will that end come? It is not a time when good and evil will be completely eradicated at once. It is a time when only the good will remain and the evil will be eliminated. That global time is coming. Before that global time comes, individuals who can govern themselves centered on good and eliminate evil must emerge. A man who has completely eliminated evil centered on good must find a woman and establish a family focused on goodness, witnessing the emergence of a family centered on good.
In the Bible, it is said that in the end times, the sheep and the goats will be separated. Why is that? What is sown will be reaped in the autumn. In other words, in the end times, we will reap according to what we have sown. Humans are sown as beings who struggle between body and mind, and this is the time when the fruits of this will manifest globally. 

When is this time? It is now, when the world is divided into democratic and communist realms. One is centered on the spiritual world, and the other is centered on the material world. One represents the inner aspect of the heart, while the other represents the outer aspect of the body. This has arisen from the fundamental struggle between body and mind. Centered around one man and one woman, it must manifest as a global fruit through the bloodline of such parents, thus appearing as a world focused on materialism and a world focused on the heart.

However, just because this has manifested does not mean it is resolved; it must be resolved. The resolution does not begin from the world. The resolution of world problems does not lead to the resolution of family problems, and the resolution of family problems does not lead to the resolution of individual problems. Today, while people around the world are pursuing a unified world, the current state of the world cannot be organized merely by addressing the resultant fruits. It cannot be organized without establishing a resolution plan centered on the originating individuals.

The unification plan proposed by the Unification Church is rooted in each individual human being. The root of our struggle between body and mind is where the issue lies. How can we deny the reality of the body, which tends toward evil, and return to a perfect person who governs everything centered on the heart that stands on the origin of goodness? The question is whether we can completely eliminate evil and return as individuals centered on goodness.

That is why religions up to now have not developed with the goal of world salvation but rather with the goal of individual salvation. People say they believe in Jesus to go to heaven or they believe in some religion to reach paradise. There is no concept of family or nation, nor is there a concept of the world. Their desires, even if vaguely, look toward the time of the world, but their ultimate goal is not world salvation; it all comes back to individual salvation.

When we ask where the cause lies, the solution is not at the end of the world but within the individual. Because it is within the individual, religions have pursued individual salvation from the standpoint of determining victory or defeat, and you must understand this.

We must lay the foundation for individuals to completely triumph centered on religion, so that through that individual, families can be completely saved, nations can be saved, and the world can be saved. To connect individual salvation with family salvation, tribal, national, and world salvation, the method for completing individual salvation must emerge, and a resolution, a formula must be established. Without that, it is impossible. So what does our Unification Church advocate? It proposes a unification plan to prevent and resolve the origin of evil centered on the individual.

Then what is the fall? It is to have broken the connection of life with God. Having broken the connection of life with God, to whom did we connect our life? We connected it with Satan. And we have fallen outside of God's realm of love. While we have fallen outside of God's realm of love, into what realm of love have we entered? We have entered into Satan's realm of love. This is the problem. Currently, your life is not centered on God but rather on Satan; it is not a life born centered on God's love but rather a life born centered on Satan's love. This is the issue. This problem must be resolved.

Today, the expectation of faith and the expectation of reality taught by the Unification Church aim to fulfill the expectation for the Messiah. What is this for? It is to strip away original sin. When original sin is stripped away, we transition into God's realm of life and love. To achieve this, what must be done? We must be grafted. To turn a wild olive tree into a true olive tree, we must cut off the wild olive tree and graft it onto the true olive tree. Similarly, to transform humans, who are like wild olive trees, into people who are like true olive trees, we must go through the process of denying oneself and then present a new affirmation, a complete affirmation. By doing so, the essence of the being will not be a wild olive tree but will become a true olive tree, and instead of being a person who is centered on good and evil, they will emerge as a person who is completely centered on goodness, forming a family, a clan, a nation, and a world centered around such a person. This is the unification plan of the Unification Church, and this is the current position that the members of the Unification Church desire.

The issue for current members of the Unification Church is how difficult it is to save one individual from evil. What is the problem for the current members of the Unification Church? It is to completely liberate ‘me’ centered on body and mind. How difficult is this, and how fierce is that struggle? This struggle cannot be compared to the competition between the U.S. and the Soviet Union. The conflict between the democratic world and the communist world is not even a problem. It is much more difficult than that. This struggle originates from our individual selves.

Just as there are two factions fighting within the individual, there are two factions within families, societies, nations, and the world. If we trace this back through genealogy, one is the individual of evil, the family of evil, the society of evil, the nation of evil, and the world of evil, while the other is the individual of goodness, the tribe of goodness, the nation of goodness, and the world of goodness. It is clearly divided. One side stands within the religious authority centered on God, while the other side stands within the material realm that denies God. That is how humans are.

There is no morality or ethics in this. If the heart's world is wide, it is wider than heaven and earth; if the heart's world is deep, it is deeper than heaven and earth. However, the body does not share this quality.

The body is limited. Therefore, it does not take long before they become bored. We see this in current trends as well. Sensory satisfaction centered on the flesh is exceedingly momentary. The sensations that the flesh feels through the five senses are limited. The joy of eating well and feeling good, that is, emotions centered around the environment, are limited. They cannot be infinite. They are not three-dimensional.

However, the peace that comes from the world of the heart, or the stimulation that comes from the heart, cannot be compared to the stimulation centered on the flesh. How vast is the heart? The size of the heart is beyond description. That is why the desires of the heart are great. Desires do not arise from the body but from the heart. So when can the heart rejoice, and where is the place for the heart to rejoice? It is on a different dimension from simply eating well and living well, which the body pursues. The desires of the body and the desires of the heart

The one who acts in a way that incurs a loss is the good one. This is the conclusion. Therefore, you must clearly understand the criteria for good and evil.

When trying to walk the path of goodness, you must not use others for your own benefit. Look for good people among those who seek to use others. the universe will continue to be in conflict, and thus the struggle must persist. 

Therefore, we must understand that the strength of the front line is limited by the individual’s capacity to withstand the enemy’s offensive. In such a prolonged struggle, whether it lasts for a year, ten years, a century, or even several centuries, the challenges become even greater. If the battle can be resolved within a single lifetime, it may seem manageable, but the reality is that even after one victory, the fight continues, and the relative power dynamics do not diminish. 

In this context, it is essential to recognize that the unity of the front and rear is crucial for overcoming the enemy. Just as South Korea and North Korea are in a confrontational relationship, nations that harbor animosity towards each other will find themselves in a cycle of conflict. If both sides perceive weaknesses in each other and act on them, they may remain in a stagnant state until they inevitably clash, resulting in mutual depletion rather than progress.

Thus, the question arises: which individuals or nations will endure after such confrontations? The answer lies in how united the front and rear are. When the enemy's front and rear are unified, they possess a strength that surpasses mere numbers. If a nation stands firm under a strong and united front and rear, it can withstand any attack from the enemy. Even if the enemy approaches with a force of 100, if the combined strength of the defending nation exceeds that, the enemy will ultimately fail.

The principle of strength dictates that power flows from the strong to the weak. A nation cannot be deemed strong if only its front line is robust; the rear must also be fortified. A weak front can be supported by a strong rear, but if the front is strong yet the rear is weak, the front will falter without support, leading to the nation’s downfall. This principle is fundamental and cannot be overlooked.

This applies to any organization as well. In the Unification Church, for example, there is a clear distinction between the front and rear. We are acutely aware of the many adversaries that challenge us today. We feel their attacks in our cells, emotions, and daily lives.

Therefore, when faced with opposition, the crucial question is how strong we can stand in our current environment. Will we retreat when confronted one-on-one with the enemy, or will we be able to push forward despite their strength? 

Moreover, even if we are weak, do we have a strong rear that can support us against opposing forces? If our rear is significantly stronger than the adversary’s, we can always receive reinforcement and maintain a position of mutual support. Thus, even if we appear weak on the front line, we are not truly weak if we have a powerful rear backing us up. 

In conclusion, while having the strength to defeat an enemy on the front line is ideal, it is imperative to understand that a strong rear is essential when that is not possible.
When we say we are connected, we must have the underlying connections that allow us to connect ourselves with the world. If we are not connected to the background that can provide us with the power to face the world, claiming that we can endure this global struggle and achieve victory is nothing but delusion.

The history of humanity is a history of the struggle between good and evil. When we look at the process of returning to the history of humanity today, we know that since the day good and evil confronted each other, good has been fighting against evil. In terms of the ratio of good and evil, evil is prevalent in the whole, while good starts from a spirit that is not even one. This is the main current of the struggle between good and evil today.

No matter how good God is, because He has not been able to establish a foundation on this earth, which has become entirely evil, He is seeking one man and one woman who can unite with good. Therefore, they must form a family in complete unity, establish a point of victory, and create a family that can align with good, a tribe that can align with good, a nation that can align with good, and a world that can align with good—because the world of evil has emerged, we must create a world that can correspond to it and align with good. Without resolving this issue in the struggle between the world of evil and the world of good, we cannot hope for the victory of the good world. Even if the children gathered here cannot take on the responsibility of front-line soldiers, let them have the burning desire to take on double or triple the responsibility as those in the rear.

Let us become good sons and daughters who protect the front and rear against Satan and comfort You, Father, and may we become the owners of this nation who can inherit the eternal kingdom and world from You, and may we become the ancestors of this nation.

Please personally oversee this day. We earnestly ask that You accept everything according to Your will and receive glory, and we earnestly pray and ask all these things in the name of True Parents. Amen.
