Our Responsibility
<Prayer> Beloved Father, we sincerely thank You for granting us this precious time. 

The children present here are those who have vowed to dedicate their lives to You and have resolved to put it into practice. Now, humbly bowing before You, we wish to reflect on the ‘I’ that vowed to work for myself in the past, the ‘I’ that is in the present, and the ‘I’ that must be guaranteed before the future purpose, seeking Your correct judgment and guidance. We bow before You at this time, so please, compassionate Father, let Your infinite love be with our humble hearts. Awaken us with Your love for the future generations, so that we may live meaningful lives toward the place where Your will desires us to be. We ask that all that we have be allowed to be offered as true offerings before You.

All the circumstances and desires that humans wish for tend to be centered around themselves. Because they speak and live centered on themselves, they have become beings who cannot escape this framework. When we think about how today’s ‘I’ is a form that cannot be with heaven, we must realize that we cannot discover or meet You without living in a way that contradicts a life centered on ourselves. We must feel how unforgivable our lives and environments have been before You as we navigate through the fallen world.

In such an environment, we must understand that You want to restore us a thousand times and ten thousand times, and that You have come out with a desperate heart to lead us, who do not want to leave this path. We did not know that the more ignorant humanity is in front of such efforts, the more Your sorrow is compounded.

As we reflect on our past at this time, we must realize that every time we discover ourselves unable to transcend our own boundaries, we are in a position that cannot be accepted before heaven, and we must have the humble hearts of boys and girls who can expose and confess that. Otherwise, we must think that we are beings living among the sentient beings on this earth, and as one of them, we ask You, Father, to look down upon us, the humble children.

We must understand that without forming a connection where our hearts can collide with Your heart of love, we cannot rely on You and live on this earth. Among the 30 million people, Your children gathered here have not forgotten this. When we think about this, we must clearly understand that the greater Your desire is, the more You shed tears with us, even if there are many people living on this earth.

We must know that You have come out today on behalf of humanity, struggling to overcome human ignorance, and if there are those who are struggling to become filial sons and daughters before You, please grant them a millionfold blessing, protect them with Your grace, and let them participate in Your holy and glorious place. Allow them to be Your sons and daughters who will never again be taken away by Satan.

We know well that no one can guarantee our lives. Not even the friends we believed in can guarantee our lives, nor can the spouses with whom we share vows and lives guarantee our lives. Even the most beloved parents cannot guarantee our lives, and when we think that we ourselves are also insufficient beings who cannot guarantee our lives, where will we entrust our lives today? 

While people may respond that they will live centered on their strength, will, and firm intentions, we must realize that life is a journey that begins in emptiness and ends in emptiness. When there is someone who discovers the Father who worries about all things, entrusts their lives to the Father, and offers everything before the Father, even if that appearance seems unhappy, they must feel that they are indeed happy.

Father, a small number of Your children have gathered here. Now we must dedicate our lives entirely as Yours. It must be offered not as ‘my’ or ‘his’ but as Yours. We must realize that we cannot become those who can discover ourselves as liberated and empowered unless we are allowed to be those who can discover ourselves as such. 

We must become true beings who can comfort the Father, who comes with a gentle yet earnest heart, and who can say that Your daughter and son have been waiting for You, even though we have passed through many life paths but have not had such a moment. We must realize that it was wrong to think we would serve You in the place of joy and glory.

In this context, it is essential to recognize that the concept of luck or fortune is not merely about superficial success or immediate gratification. Instead, it should be viewed through the lens of responsibility and the fulfillment of one's duties. Each individual, whether as a husband, a father, or a citizen, must strive to embody the values and principles that contribute to the greater good of their family and society.

When we speak of wishing for good fortune, we must consider the implications of that wish. It should not be a fleeting desire for personal gain but rather a commitment to uphold the dignity and honor of our roles. This means being aware of the responsibilities that come with our positions and striving to fulfill them to the best of our abilities.

As we navigate our lives, we must also be mindful of the interconnectedness of our actions and the impact they have on those around us. You may know the proverb, "A tower built with effort does not collapse." It means that those who wish to reap without sowing are foolish. When we think of the natural law that we reap what we sow, our life journey is the same. In doing good, one must have a clear purpose; only then will the desired results manifest. A person who acts with good intentions but fluctuates in their purpose from one day to the next, no matter how many good deeds they perform, will not bring about good results. This is the issue at hand.

When performing good deeds, one must focus on the nation, saying, "To save the nation, this is the path it must take. The people of the nation must be guided in this way." With a thorough mindset, whether it is thirty million people or the land of the nation, one must perform good deeds with a heart that loves the nation more than anyone else. Whether done today, tomorrow, during the day, or at night, it will all be for the nation.

Each individual has only one unique characteristic. Furthermore, each person's disposition is different. Therefore, the life goals that each person desires are not the same. Humans are born with a purpose, and as long as they exist, they will undoubtedly strive to achieve that purpose. The value of that purpose will become the utmost center for that person.

If God exists, He desires for humans to be perfect and to bear fruit from the highest value, rather than to stand in a deficient position constrained by any environmental factors. When we think of the heavenly desire for a perfect and flawless result, if we center our lives around that attainable goal, eating for that purpose, living for that purpose, acting for that purpose, and loving for that purpose, then the joy of a day will not flow away with our daily lives but will remain as eternal joy.

If one encounters sorrow in such a position, it is not sorrow caused by oneself but sorrow arising from a conflict at the place where the purpose is directed. Since the motivation for that sorrow is not oneself but the nation, it does not cause one to retreat but rather becomes a relative stimulus that allows one to reaffirm their resolve.

From this perspective, even if there is sorrow in the journey of living a life dedicated to a purpose, that sorrow does not end as mere sorrow; rather, it can become a catalyst that promotes hope for tomorrow and a new purpose for tomorrow. You must understand that there is a way to transform that sorrow into a foundation that can bring hope and blessings for tomorrow.

Human Heart

There are times when you evaluate people, saying, "This person is good. That person is bad." In such cases, what is the basis for saying someone is good? What position and what environment are you speaking from? When we consider this, the criteria are vague. Today, this land is filled with people living by such vague standards. Here, if a person smiles in the morning and smiles in the evening, no matter how much they seem good, if that goodness does not relate to a consistent purpose, it will be like a flower that blooms for a moment and then withers away. From this perspective, what will remain at the end of such a life? It will be a pitiful life that can only bring about illusory results.

Then, what position should I assert myself in to become a changed person? Should I respect myself based on the position of my family? This is the issue. If someone criticizes you with just one word, you feel bad about it. The feeling of being upset depends on the position from which you are feeling it, and it can vary greatly.

When someone says, "Our Unification Church teacher is coming this evening; let's go see," some may respond, "Oh, really? Let's go," and come with a good feeling, while others may not feel the same way. That is the problem.

People like big things. Do you like big things? Yes. They like big things, but it is not easy to become something big. However, many people have the mindset of wanting something big to just fall into their laps. South Korea is referred to as the "three-thousand-ri peninsula." Is South Korea big or small? If South Korea were only ten thousand ri, would you not want more? Anyone who does not wish for South Korea to be the biggest in the world is not a citizen of South Korea. They are a traitor, a national disgrace. Yet, you would not feel bad about this. You cannot protest against it, can you? The fact that you are not angry shows this.

Then, do you want South Korea to be the biggest while you remain at the bottom? You want South Korea to grow while you stand at the top. This is human nature. You wish for such grand things, yet you find yourself in a pitiful state. You may feel bad about hearing this, but it is true. You want South Korea to be the best in the world, but you also have the desire for it to happen centered around yourself. Those who do not have this desire would not be able to speak even if they were beaten to death. (Laughter) Isn't that strange? It is indeed strange. Sometimes when you look in the mirror, you realize that you are not worthy of such desires, yet your heart wishes for it. This is a curious matter.

The autumn in Korea is truly beautiful. The autumn sky in Korea is something to be proud of to the world. The clear autumn sky is high and endless. However, your heart wishes to be even higher and wider than that. Isn't that true? Yes, it is. I feel the same way. Looking at it this way, it seems you resemble me. (Laughter) I do not know whether I resemble you or you resemble me, but in any case, we are alike.

Humans Resembling God

But ultimately, who do people resemble to become who they are? They resemble their father. Then, who does your father resemble to be like that? He resembles his parents. If you keep going up the line, you reach the ancestors of humanity. Because human ancestors are like that, we are like this. Then, who do the ancestors of humanity resemble to have become like that? This is the question. It is because there is a master who created humans in that way.

A work of art is created because the artist had a vision for that work. Is that not the case? I doubt anyone would deny this. Therefore, whom do people inevitably resemble? They resemble their parents. If they do not resemble their parents, it means that the characteristics of several generations of ancestors are hidden and combined with the traits of the mother and father to create a human being. It is not that they emerged from a place with no origin or connection.

You may think you are becoming who you are by yourself, but many of your ancestors have come and gone. Let’s not speak poorly of those thousands of generations of ancestors; let’s call them "bosses." You, as an individual, are the result of the combined essence of all those many bosses. Do you feel good hearing this? This is the wonderful nature of being human.

Because of this, you are like a collection of various forms, qualifications, and values from thousands and tens of thousands of generations of ancestors, akin to exhibits displayed in a museum. This is the appearance that you present today. Our ancestors have set us up as exhibits before the world, saying, "This is what our descendants are like." Have you thought about it this way? There may be many men and women in this world, but when you look at an individual, that person is born as the fruit of the totality of their ancestors.

If there is a heaven or spiritual realm as religions say, the spirits of your ancestors would be there, watching over you without dying. Would those ancestors wish for their children and grandchildren to do poorly or well? "They wish for them to do well." How well do you think they wish for them to do? They would wish for them to be the best in the world. If they wish for them to be the best in the world, would they only want them to be the president of the world? If there is someone greater than the president of the world, they would want their grandchildren to be the most beloved children of that person. It cannot be otherwise.

Do your grandparents love their grandchildren? "Yes." As they age, they get wrinkles, their hands and faces become wrinkled, and their hair turns gray. Grandfathers even have beards. Additionally, older people may have a smell. Despite this, when their grandchildren come, they find them adorable and want to hug and caress them, even if the grandchildren run away saying they do not like it. Still, grandparents love their grandchildren so much that they buy them bread. I have felt this emotion too. Have you not felt it? Even if the grandchildren say they do not like it, the grandparents follow them around trying to help. Would those grandparents hate their descendants after they pass away? Think about it. Would they love them or hate them? You would feel good if your ancestors loved you, wouldn’t you? 

However, if your ancestor were a murderer or a robber, would you feel good? How would you think then? If you have a distinguished ancestor, you would boast about it, right? Even elementary school or kindergarten children would brag that President Park is their ancestor, saying, "Wow! Park is the president now, so Park is the best." They would say that even if there is no direct relation.

There is no limit to discussing this. In any case, whom do you resemble? You resemble your ancestors. If there is a sculpture or a literary work, it has emerged from the vision conceived in the heart of the artist. Is that not so? If an artist wants to encompass the world, the work is born from that desire. Isn’t that the case? No matter how much you deny it, it is an undeniable fact.

When do people like or dislike something? 

I, too, did not initially like calling on God. In reality, I had to call on Him because I could not help it. I am not someone who calls on God blindly. I have examined, prayed, dissected, tasted, thrown, and listened, and when I found that there was no other option, I concluded that it had to be God. I did not set out to become a religious leader from the beginning. I may have had a nature that liked God, but it was not a blind liking. So why do I like God? It is because God is absolutely good. That is the conclusion I have reached. Conversely, why do people dislike God? It is because they are positioned in a situation where they cannot help but dislike Him.

So, when do people like something? They like it when they meet someone with whom their hearts resonate. What happens if a woman is alone? She dies within a hundred years. She fails. However, when there is a man, for some reason, a force that attracts the subject arises. The same goes for men; when there is a target, a force that can lift them up emerges. When there is no relationship between subject and object, does that force arise? It does not.

When you are a man, did you know that there is a woman when you were born, or did you not know? Young male students, did you know or not? When you consider this, you cannot deny the existence of God. You may not have known, but He did.

Therefore, every existence must have a relationship between subject and object. They must work together to achieve a combined purpose that brings about results greater than the value of either the subject or the object. To make that purpose possible through power, there must first be a subject and an object. When there is a subject and an object, the results can transform into something greater.

This is only true in the world of love. The world of power is the opposite. Do you understand? 

Thus, the universe was created through correspondence and conflict. This conflict does not exist to destroy what corresponds but is a means to protect and nurture what corresponds. If this is understood, the fundamental issues of the universe can be resolved. However, this has become a problem, and communists have been causing confusion in the world with their dialectics and so on. In fact, this is a difficult concept, so some may understand it while others may not.

Is there anyone who has received true love and wishes to live apart from it? How can this happen? All beings in the universe are protected and nurtured because when one individual diminishes, another individual simultaneously becomes the opposite. Therefore, for humans, this action is centered around love, which can achieve more ideal purposes, seeking the greater weighted purpose of the larger world. For a nation to prosper, each citizen must have a patriotic spirit that loves the nation, right? For friends to accomplish something together, they must be united in friendship, right? Similarly, for the world to prosper, humanity must have a spirit of philanthropy.

Before there is power, what must exist? "Love." It has been said that love must exist. However, if there is no subject and object, power does not arise. Shall I share a relatable story about this? When you are alone, does power arise? When you eat alone and feel full and good, does power arise when you sit quietly? Anyone who claims to have power alone is a mad person. Power arises when you exercise. That is because you are exercising with a counterpart.

When you feel good or bad, it is not just about yourself. You must remember this well. When I say I feel bad or good, what is the reason? I feel bad when I am invaded, and I feel good when I can benefit. It is simple. I feel bad when I suffer a loss, and I feel good when I am in a position to gain. 

If the body acts as it wishes, it becomes a failure.
You must have seen many people walking in Myeongdong, Seoul, every day. Those people all think the same thing when they leave their homes in the morning: they hope for good fortune today. Is there anyone who goes out thinking they will suffer a loss, even if just a little? There is not a single person like that. If there were, they would be considered crazy. Similarly, the action of power works the same way. It never acts in situations where there is a loss. You need to understand this.

If you conduct an experiment with ionic bonds of elements, you will see that when there are positive or negative ions, it seems like any ion with opposite charges would bond, but that is not the case. Upon closer inspection, only the ions that correspond to each other will bond. If there is even a tiny benefit to one, it will rush to bond with the other. Everything operates this way.

So why does it work this way? It is because both people and God are like that. Since everything in the material world, down to every molecule and atom, is created by such a being, they exhibit this kind of action.

Therefore, when we say that power acts, it means that the subject and the object are meeting and exchanging with each other. From this perspective, does your conscience act or not? When we consider whether conscience becomes the subject or the object, does the fact that conscience acted imply that there is a subject and an object, or that there is none? It implies that there is one. So who is that subject? We do not know. But we know it exists. Just as a compass points north when it is at the North Pole, and points south when at the South Pole, the fact that our conscience acts proves that our conscience is either in a subjective position or an objective position.

When you look at the world with a united heart in that love, it is already within you. Why? Because what was thought in God's heart was created, it is within you. That is why figures like Buddha reached such a state and realized the truth of "In heaven and on earth, I alone exist." Even when looking at a handkerchief left by a beloved wife as she dies, even if it is worth only fifty cents, one would say they will look at it until they die and find joy in life. Isn't that so? It is more precious than their own life. If a simple handkerchief presented as a condition of human love is like this, how much more precious is something that has an unchanging condition in God's love? Once you have that, you cannot help but dance.

Reverend Moon of the Unification Church has reached such a level that no matter how much the world makes noise, it does not matter. In time, everyone will know who is great. You must completely deny the world. You must deny everything.

So the question is, in what position do you find joy? If there is a path you want to take for your whole life, you must put all your sincerity into finding that path. If someone has poured all their energy into creating a precious work, and then war breaks out and they have to evacuate, would they leave that work behind and flee, or would they take it with them? They would hold onto it even at the moment of death. If that is the case for a person, how much more so for God, who created humans as His greatest masterpiece? Would God feel bored after a hundred years of creating and say, "Ah, I’m tired of this," and throw it away?

Love is eternal and true. When people talk about love, they say, "Oh, my beloved, I can love you for a lifetime!" Yes, they say, "I can love you forever!" But would God, after living for about a hundred years, want to throw it away? Because God is the absolute being, the object of His love is also absolute. Since He possesses eternal attributes, once He loves, He wants to love forever, doesn’t He? "He would want to love forever." Therefore, it concludes that humans must also follow the law of love and cannot be anything less than eternal. No matter how much you discuss the details, it is still insufficient. Do you understand why it must be this way? Because love is meant to be eternal. Is there anyone who wishes to live with their husband for about a hundred years and then die? They want to live forever. This is true for both humans and God. Eternal life comes only from love.

It resembles God. So why do they strive to reach the very top, unable to go higher or lower? It is to be a plus in front of the absolute subject.

Would it be fun for God to be alone at the highest position? No, it wouldn’t be. God is no exception. If God is alone at the top, what fun would that be? No matter how small the object, it holds absolute value before God. What this means is that if an object is placed before the absolute being, it possesses absolute value.

A child must surpass their father.

Our Unification Church members will create people who are better than Jesus. However, we are criticized as heretics. What is a heretic? They are the ones who are orthodox, and we are the heretics. When autumn comes, those who prepare their hearts to welcome spring will develop and grow. Dead people, even if it becomes autumn, do not prepare to welcome spring. They do not prepare to welcome spring. However, trees, when autumn comes and leaves fall, begin to prepare for spring. Do you understand? You must understand that. No matter how cold winter comes and the biting winds blow, we must endure to welcome the new spring. Even if we face great persecution, that is not a problem. We must have the confidence to drop the anchor of life in the midst of adversity. To do this, we must deny ourselves.

What do you want to be for God? Do you want to be a servant of God, an adopted child, or do you want to be true sons and daughters? "We want to be true sons and daughters." Even if our faces are not handsome, everyone wants to become God's sons and daughters. This is a question that does not even need to be asked. Anyone who asks is childish. If we become God's sons and daughters, will we be the eldest son or daughter, or the youngest son or daughter? "We will be the eldest." Then, as the eldest, what should we do when our father passes away? We must take on the responsibility of our father on both shoulders, save our younger siblings before we live, and even if we die, we must save our younger siblings. In doing so, we become the perfect eldest daughter and eldest son that no one in history can take that position from.

Jesus, who came as God's only begotten son, had to bear that responsibility, but our ancestors said, 'I don't want to.' Because of this shirking of responsibility, there has been no perfect eldest daughter and eldest son until now. There has been only one person in this universe who has come like that, and that person is Jesus, who did not marry until he was over 30 years old. He was born as the son of a carpenter, doing nothing remarkable, just chopping wood and whittling. However, Jesus held the heart that 'God is my Father.' He had the mindset that 'the God who created heaven and earth is not the father of someone else but my father!' How much determination did he have? Just because he made a decision once does not mean it settled in his heart. So think about how much he must have immersed himself until that determination settled in Jesus' heart.

The devil confused him so that he could not think that way, the surrounding environment was negative, and they tried to kill him. However, Jesus said, 'Even if I die, the God I hold onto is undoubtedly my Father. If I cannot prove this, I will prove it through my death.' And he said, 'The son is a son, but he is the only begotten son.' This means there is only one son, Jesus.

Then does this mean that Jesus is going to take full responsibility for God's affairs, or not? If God does nothing, is it saying that he will take God's place, or not? "He will take God's place." So Satan said, 'Hey, you! Are you the only begotten son of God? It is God's will to save the world, so try saving this fallen world. Experience how much pain it brings!' and subjected him to all kinds of trials and persecutions. It was a path of death, but Jesus remained steadfast. 'Come, death! Even if you block my way with a sword threatening my life, I will walk this path of purpose. I will surely win, even if I have to give my life. As long as no one works harder than me, I am undoubtedly God's firstborn.' He sacrificed his life and died with that mindset. And when the enemies pierced his heart with a spear, he prayed, "Father, forgive them, for they do not know what they are doing." (Luke 23:34) What a wonderful prayer this is! He reached a level that humans cannot even conceive. I cannot express how magnificent his actions were as a man. Think about it. How amazing is that? A man must transcend life and death to reach that level.

Today, men in the world foolishly take girls to play in the mountains. Those guys are the ones who, when they are about to die, will pray not to die. Every single one of them is like that. When I see such people, I want to say, 'Die.' People who have come into the world with a purpose cannot be like that. If parents oppose the purpose, it is 'Die.' When I look at all of this, I do not think I am inferior to Jesus. Because Christianity does not accept it today, I cannot unfold that content through Christianity. Therefore, while I have made it difficult for our Unification Church members, upon reflection, it was a good thing. Unification Church members have walked the path of suffering, but that path is not a path where life intersects; it is a more progressive path of life.

So will we become the eldest son and eldest daughter? "We will." When God says, 'I will let you do it alone. I will make you the eldest son and eldest daughter,' will we do it or not? Do we need to do it as Unification Church members? "We need to." Those who want to do it, raise your hands. Put them down. There is no need to ask such things.

The district leader came to me and said, 'Teacher, the Unification Church is in big trouble. Please help us just a little.' Did the district leader do well or not? Answer me. We must discern right from wrong; did he do well or not? "He did not." Then how can we become the eldest son and eldest daughter? "We cannot." Not being able to is the principle.

How desperate must a person be to rely on others and stretch out their hands for help? In the Unification Church, we must not think that way. I have come this far with my bare hands, but I have never thought of relying on others. Even now, that thought has not changed. If I make someone indebted to me, I will do so, but I will not seek to be indebted. Do not become a Unification Church member who relies on others. Looking at the young people today, they seem to have lost their minds. Even when blessings are given, they do not follow. When a newcomer hears this, they cannot feel bad. They cannot even curse. The person cursing is not bad; the person saying such things is not bad. Therefore, everyone must make a firm resolution.

Even if I see someone fighting while walking, I do not just watch. After knowing right from wrong, I cannot remain silent. Even if legs are broken and heads are cracked, I must make a judgment on right and wrong. I possess that kind of character. Do not be too fond of the district leader. When has the district leader ever kicked women out while pushing them? Never, right? At that time, women must be stubborn. They must say, 'District leader, come out!' and drag him around. Even if they say they do not want to, they must drag him around for the church to develop. To become the eldest son among sons and the eldest daughter among daughters, that is what must be done.

If we fulfill the mission of sons and daughters from the same position, to whom will God give the inheritance rights? The inheritance rights are given to the eldest son and eldest daughter. It is unavoidable. Therefore, you must have the disposition to receive God's inheritance rights. Jacob was wise. He did not hesitate and received the blessing before his brother. Hesitating leads to many losses.

During our joint blessing ceremony, there were about 250 applicants this time. We ask the young men and women in front of us questions. Then they choose three people they like. We explain that this man has this character, and your character is like this, so this character matches and that character does not. When we suggest changing partners, most people wonder, 'How can the teacher know me when he sees me for the first time?' and cannot answer. At that time, a person must have decisiveness. They must hurry. There is no time to think. However, if the judgment is delayed, everything will be taken away without a trace.

Some women subtly watch the teacher's reactions. They think, 'Will the teacher think I match with that person or not?' and there are people who try to curry favor with the teacher. Then the teacher first asks, 'Do you like that person?' If they say, 'I am not sure. Please take responsibility for me,' it means they do not feel that bad. So, we analyze whether they feel bad or good. However, if they say they do not like it, that person will undoubtedly be taken away. Therefore, the teacher decides that you should meet this kind of person because of your character and that kind of person because of your character. If it is even slightly better than what they think, they will accept it.

That is why you must think carefully about this. You should prepare what to ask from ten years ago. Do you understand what I mean? And Unification Church members must not fail to handle what has been given to them. A young man or woman preparing for the blessing may find the partner chosen by the teacher acceptable, but if they say they do not like it, they will be in trouble. If they make excuses and say they do not like it, then the teacher will not be able to do anything. Is marriage conducted like an auction? The teacher hates that very much. Once you enter the blessing ceremony and the teacher makes a decision, that is it. However, if you say you do not like it and then get caught by the teacher, whether you are old or young, the teacher will not forgive you. The teacher's heart is infinitely good when it is good. But look into the teacher's eyes. What happens? When things go wrong, there is no forgiveness. Do you understand? "Yes."

Therefore, if you are going to become something, become God's eldest daughter. Even if you cannot get married, become the eldest daughter. Do you understand? If the eldest daughter gets married first, can the younger daughter get married? No, she cannot. So, the younger siblings must get married first, and the eldest daughter and eldest son must get married last. And even if you buy a house, you must buy your younger siblings' houses first. Then, later, if you all come together to buy my house, I would not ask for anything more. If you become such a person, you will forever be the eldest son and eldest daughter of that family. That is the principle of heaven.

If you judge good and bad based on yourselves, what kind of judgment will that be? And can I become someone who can judge all matters from any position and live with some hope? If there is an absolute being at the center of the universe, I must be in a position where I have fulfilled the mission of the eldest son and the mission of the eldest daughter before that absolute being.

Prepare for hardship and trials. 

Will there be no persecution on the path he takes? Will there be no tears on the path he takes? Will there be no slander on the path he takes? Will there be no arrows from enemies flying towards him? Will there be no traps on his path? There will be all of that. We must understand that there are many obstacles on our path, like steep mountains, as we face the difficult moments of history when any nation on this earth is about to perish. However, we must accept it as our fate and say, 'I must go this way.' We must not complain about our fate. We must not face our fate while crying over it; we must be able to accept it joyfully.

You must understand that there is no happiness or satisfaction in your complaints and grievances. Let’s assume a couple who fled from North Korea has prepared a small room in a corner of the neighborhood. They live in a room where it is just right for two people to lie down, but they do not think of it as hardship; they know it as happiness and become a source of comfort for those who come and go. They greet the elderly, saying, 'Hello, grandfather! How have you been? How do you feel today? May you be comfortable tomorrow as well.' They always live with smiles, becoming the talk of the town. At first, they may be indifferent, but as time passes, they will become interested.

Then, the poor and unhappy will come to consult with them. They will ask, 'What is so good about you two that you smile every day?' At that time, if they say, 'I realized that there is no happiness or satisfaction in complaints and grievances. I learned that heaven opens up in a heart of gratitude, and everything is fulfilled in a heart of gratitude. So, we decided to live with smiles,' that person will also accept it.

Therefore, even if the path of death approaches me, I must accept it gratefully. I must be able to gratefully accept that I can overcome ten deaths with this one. I can atone for ten deaths with this one. The founder of the Unification Church, Reverend Moon, has been to prison many times. He has not missed a single prison, from the Japanese prison to the communist prison. He is an expert on prisons. (Laughter) And when he goes to prison, he knows how to give discipline. He gives discipline to the Japanese, saying, 'You are like my child, so I will make sure you do not come back.' If we catch people doing bad things in this world, we will surely discipline them. (The recording was briefly interrupted.)

Even if the established churches oppose and persecute us in our progress, we Unification Church members will not be discouraged or retreat. We have come this far. Looking back, those times were truly fun, filled with dramatic scenes and thrills. Even among close friends, it is fun to play pranks. Sitting around seriously and talking about boring things is not fun. That is why people occasionally need fresh stimulation. Therefore, those who joined the church before the age of 30 will be made to suffer greatly under my hand. If you do not want to suffer, do not join. Do not do silly things like carrying the established church pastor's bag. I may have come here for the first time today, but I feel the most uncomfortable when invited to a feast.
I think it is pretty. The teacher does not like to invite others to a feast where they would owe a favor, but rather prefers to invite them to a gathering. You should also be like that. You must make others owe you. Do you understand?

The Path of Loyal Subjects and Filial Sons
We have come to know the way to become sons and daughters of God. So, can I truly become a son or daughter of God? The answer is simple. God has been carrying out the providence of restoration for 6,000 years, and it is still not complete. God has been doing this for a long time, but our lives must take a path of effort that is many times greater. You must understand this. Therefore, the path of a loyal subject cannot be an easy one. Once a person takes on the name of a loyal subject, they must live for heaven to receive that title from heaven. The path of a filial son is the same. Therefore, how precious and valuable it is. Everything I eat, I must eat for that purpose; everything I see, I must see for that purpose; everything I say, I must say for that purpose; and everything I do, I must do for that purpose. Even if that path is one of sorrow and tears, I must take on the path that the heavenly Lord God must walk, and we must understand that we have the responsibility to fulfill the duties of a filial son and a loyal subject. Even if I have to fall to the ground, blocking the path of God's tears, I must walk that path again. There, I must fulfill the duties of loyalty and filial piety.

No matter how much someone in the human world may mock, how a nation may betray, or how a group may attack, the problem lies in not being able to walk that path, and in not being able to find it, so we must understand that only that problem remains. Furthermore, when we look back at the past, we must reflect on what we could not do and dedicate our lives to moving forward for that purpose, and then we will walk a path that no one in the heavenly world has ever walked, as claimed by the founder of the Unification Church. Do you understand?

The Path of Religion
Think quietly for a moment. Today, we humans have fallen. Therefore, you should call upon all your ancestors, and if there are any good ancestors among them, ask them. “Before you claim to be my unparalleled good ancestor, who stands in a glorious position, did you have a nation you could love, a sovereignty you could love, and a people you could love? Did you love the nation you were born into, the sovereignty you were born into, and the people you were born into, or did you love the nation, sovereignty, and people that God can guarantee and prove? Have you ever stood in such a position? Have you ever met the good parents that God wants to establish?” When you ask these questions, those ancestors will not be able to answer. And when you ask, “Have you ever met the ideal good parents that heaven and earth can establish, and have you ever received praise as a perfect son of God?”

Where will you find the nation that your ancestors could not find, and where will you meet and love the people that your ancestors could not love again, and where will you go to reclaim the sovereignty that your ancestors could not find? This is the path that humanity must collectively seek for one purpose. If God exists, isn’t this a responsibility that God must fulfill together with humanity? Therefore, we must turn our eyes to that and devote our hearts to earnestly seek it out.

However, the Republic of Korea is not the nation we are looking for, nor is the United States, nor is the Soviet Union. Countless ancestors have searched for an ideal world throughout their lives in the historical process, but there has never been an ancestor who could realize the ideals of good parents, good families, good nations, good sovereignty, and a good world centered around the homeland that the heart can long for. No matter how much responsibility they took on, they could not fulfill that responsibility.

In this light, among the approximately 3 billion humans living on this earth, have we humans had the background to love our brothers, relatives, and tribes from our homeland? No one has that background. Because we have lost our homeland, we do not have a homeland, and because we do not have that nation, we cannot have the world of our homeland. However, we must understand that the path our hearts must take is still far away, and before us lies a path of suffering and trials. Therefore, you must overcome these difficulties and move forward.

With all your sincerity, you must become the true body of goodness that humanity desires and that heaven desires, become the parents of parents, and feel resentment for not being able to fulfill the duties of love that are the model for humanity. And after realizing that you were born with the blood of enemies, you must cast out that dirty blood and become someone who can be newly dedicated before heaven. No matter what path of suffering and persecution lies ahead, if there is a path where I can quietly walk with my true self, I must be ready to welcome death a hundred or a thousand times with joy, as this is the path we must take in our lives. In this fallen world, we cannot find this path without going through the path of injustice. This is what you must understand as the so-called path of religion.

Then, where is our homeland? The land where you were born is not your homeland, but the land of enemies, the land of resentment, the land of sorrow, the land of Satan, and the land of ruin, so you must understand that the nation established on that land is also a nation of resentment. Therefore, you must throw off the chains that bind you and seek the joy of being able to welcome your individual liberation. You must seek the joy of your family being liberated, your tribe, your nation, and the entire world being able to enjoy liberation.

However, because we were born as fallen humans, we discover that we ourselves are trapped in a prison like a fortress. Our hearts strive to break free, but our bodies have no way to break free. Struggling in this way and falling apart is the path of life. Therefore, you must understand that you too are a person who must break through that path. Thus, we must seek our homeland, find our original selves, find our original parents, find our original siblings, find our original tribes, find our original nations, and find our original world.

The Path for Unification Church Members
What is the responsibility given to the members of the Unification Church today? Have you fulfilled that responsibility? Centered on God's providence of restoration, you must become the beloved sons and daughters of God and inherit that tradition. You must have the thought that can inherit pure love, pure objects, and pure unity, and you must serve your parents in your homeland. Since you have not served your parents and have not led your relatives, you must lead your relatives, and since you have not lived in that nation with your parents, you must lead that nation, and since you have not lived in that world with your parents, you must lead that world. To do this, we must shoulder our responsibilities as frontline soldiers and do our best to overcome the trials, difficulties, and tribulations that come our way. Therefore, only those who can navigate this path can surpass the standards of liberation from the first to the eighth.

We must take on such responsibilities and, even if the world perishes, we must not perish ourselves, but look forward to liberation and move forward. This is the path that Unification Church members must understand.

Our position is that of the sons and daughters of God. We are in the position of God's eldest son and daughter. In that position, we must seek the homeland of goodness, the tribes of goodness, the nations of goodness, the sovereignty of goodness, and the world of goodness. When we establish a new tradition, if there is no subject, I must become the subject, and if there is no object, I must become the object, and even if I have to do both roles, I must achieve this and go to the restored heaven, which is the original world. In that process of restoration, we must have the conviction that we cannot die, and if we must die, we must die with a deep-rooted resentment that we can be resurrected again to resolve our grievances. The path taken by those who bear such responsibilities must be a path of struggle. It cannot be anything but a path of struggle.

Frontline soldiers are always in a situation where they are aiming their weapons at the enemy, so they never know when they might lose their lives. Therefore, do not be careless, but while fulfilling your responsibilities, if there is someone who can remain as an individual, as a family, as a tribe, as a nation, and as a citizen of the world, that person is worthy of being called the eldest son and daughter of heaven. Only then will we become sons and daughters who are not ashamed to inherit all the heavenly achievements that have been hidden in heaven and earth. To do this, I must bear the cross of all people and walk the path of suffering that everyone must endure. I must understand this as my duty and be able to appeal for the sake of all humanity to be indemnified. This is precisely the path that Jesus walked.

Only those who can shoulder all responsibilities and illuminate the historical path of righteousness in heaven and earth can be said to have fulfilled their responsibilities as members of the Unification Church. All conditions will start anew from here. The connections made here will not only be human connections but will also pass through the heavenly and eternal historical ages. With that connection, we must create a foundation that can be loyal to and respected by all humanity as a model of global liberation. Thus, we will become sons and daughters who cannot help but receive God's love in both the earthly and heavenly worlds. We must understand that this is the responsibility of the members of the Unification Church.

<Prayer> Please have compassion on your children gathered here. We have come to know through your words that the term ‘our responsibility’ has been inherited with such tremendous history. We also understand that the path of indemnity remains for the individual, family, tribe, nation, and world. However, feeling that we are far too inadequate to go forward with the rest of our lives, we must become your sons and daughters who can reflect on and blame ourselves for not fulfilling that responsibility during our youth.

Rather than avoiding the cross laid upon us, we must say that we will carry even the remaining cross, and even if it means dying while carrying it, we understand that through that one person, you can gather three people according to the heavenly principle, thus expanding the domain of the good world. We have come to know that you have carried out operations to first receive and take away, operations to multiply through death, and operations to lose oneself and seek the whole.

Today, our Unification Church must not become a Unification Church for itself. It must become a Unification Church to save the nation, and the Republic of Korea must not become a nation for itself but must become a Republic of Korea that saves the world. The world must not become a world for itself but must become a world that connects to the love of God, the origin of precious life. We must realize the tremendous fact that when the path of life for all beings is connected there, humanity can welcome joy.

We may be lowly and humble in body, but we have come to understand that behind the high and precious hearts we aspire to lies a tremendous historical connection. When we think of this, we must match our steps to the direction our hearts are aiming for, even if it means cutting off all external connections. We have come to know that this is the path we must take.

Please remember your children gathered here, and allow us to stand in the position of the object centered on the love of the Father. May we become daughters and sons who can cry out to the Father with all our hearts, and may we be those who shed tears for the Father. If there are sons and daughters who shed tears longing for the Father, please allow us to realize that those tears are not in vain.

Please do not let your little children in the Middle East have empty desires. Let them understand that all the empty desires of the world are like clouds that pass away in an instant. As we deeply feel how pitiful the Father is, who has set out to find the orphan who has lost their parents with a heart that can forget oneself while longing for the infinite original value, may we become sons and daughters who cry out and struggle toward the Father, knowing that the Father will never forsake them. We must become victorious sons and daughters who realize such a noble life and seek to become sons and daughters of the one who is the leader of the earthly and heavenly worlds, and even if there is a path of harsh suffering, we must become your sons and daughters who know how to go against that path.

We now know that the position we must stand in is that of God's eldest son and daughter. In that position, we must embrace not only our individual selves but also the world, and with the heart to save the world, we must fulfill the responsibilities of sons and daughters. Please allow us to understand that what you desire is global, and therefore it is the responsibility of sons and daughters to transcend and soar beyond this world. Even if all paths of suffering block our way, please allow us to be a group that can advance together.

Let us realize that the path of those seeking a comfortable way can be blocked at any time and anywhere. Jesus presented the paradoxical logic that “whoever seeks to preserve their life will lose it, and whoever loses it will save it” (Luke 17:33) because the source of the heavenly principle is in a position that contradicts reality. We, the members of the Unification Church in this public path, ask you to allow us to run this path vigorously. If we become weak on this path, we ask you to allow us to run to the end with the conviction that the Father will lead us.

Please take care of all circumstances of this day with your warm hand. Are there those who are weary on the path of life? Please take care of them even more. Allow us to be able to face the new holy sunlight of bright glory that we must meet tomorrow. May we discover our overflowing selves with the new morning and become sons and daughters who can worship the Father with joy as individuals who can praise the infinite value.

May we be those who can hear the voice calling us to welcome this remaining world and run toward it, and even if that journey is tiring, may we be your sons and daughters who can endure and overcome. At this time, through all the words we have shared, may we take one more step toward the Father.
I thank you for allowing us to approach you and embrace your heart, Father. I earnestly ask that this time be an opportunity for us to advance further in the connections granted by you in this world, so please oversee everything. I pray in the name of the True Parents. Amen. *

5) True Path of Life
─ Words from the Jongno District Tour Meeting ─
<Prayer> Fallen humanity has gone through countless twists and turns in the process of weaving history. As we look upon humanity, which has lived in sighs, despair, and lamentation, we must once again feel how much suffering and hardship our Father has endured. 

We need to reflect on the relationship between humanity and the Father, and how the Father has worked tirelessly to awaken the people on this earth who do not understand the connections made with humanity, bringing them to the position of servants. We must also think about how much humanity has betrayed the true love of the Father, who has pioneered the path of adoption to inherit all His possessions and enterprises to the children of the enemy.

Moreover, you have restored us to the position of true children, leading us to the original world that you have longed for. Therefore, you are the Father of all humanity. Please help us realize this marvelous grace that has allowed us to have the status of children.

Father, your children have gathered here this evening. We reflect on the past days when we longed to meet but could not. Please bless this time we have to meet the children in the Jongno District. Although it seems that we are connected through humanity, it is not so. 

Since February 15, 1971 (Monday), Jongno Church. * This message was given during the night tour of the nine districts in Seoul at the Jongno District headquarters.

As we look forward to the fulfillment of the wishes of all humanity, we have endured and walked the path of death, continuing the connections of heaven. When we think about how we have come to stand in a position where we can serve the Father due to these connections today, we must recognize how much effort the Father has put in behind the scenes without our knowledge.

The individual that appears here may seem extremely weak and lacking, but through the ancestors behind us, we have gathered in this one place, transcending distances and numerous connections. We sincerely thank you for this amazing grace that allows us to experience the heart of the Father in this one place.

Even though there is only one place on this earth where we can form a new connection to admire the homeland we lost thousands of years ago, when we think about the fact that this connection has been established through insignificant beings like us, it becomes a source of pride for us and our nation. However, we appear too insignificant in front of the great efforts you have made, so please have compassion for our pitiful situation.

Now we must possess the heart of a child who has nothing. Just as a child longs for their mother's milk, let us have a sincere heart that seeks the path of life. Regardless of age, we must become like children before our parents, and similarly, we must become like children before the Father. According to our individual circumstances and environments, please provide us with the gifts of life so that we may be abundantly filled during this time. Since you have granted us this precious time, please bestow upon us special grace.

May each of our hearts be immersed in the great love and mercy that comes from the Father, and may this be a holy time where we can experience the wonderful circumstances, sorrows, and feelings of the Father. 

Let this time be entirely under the Father's dominion. Please do not allow any forces of darkness to leave their mark here, and may this be a time where we can completely uproot the seeds of sin with your fiery gaze. Thus, may the connections we wish to establish with the Father be formed here, making this time a day of resurrection in our lives that we can never forget, and a day of pride in our faith journey that can illuminate our lives. 

Through this time, may you find your beloved children, share the hidden feelings, and convey the deeply buried stories, allowing precious connections to be formed among us. I earnestly hope and wish for this.

Please oversee this gathering according to the time you have permitted. May the hearts of the messenger and the recipients align solely with your circumstances, and may we ourselves be deeply moved by your desires, captured by all the realms you govern, and unite ourselves on the foundation of your holy grace. Father, I earnestly ask you to take charge.

I ask you to oversee everything personally, and I pray in the name of the True Parents. Amen.

<Words> As we go through our faith life, there are many questions that arise, and many things we want to know. There may be doubts about whether God exists. How wonderful it would be if we could directly ask God these questions and discuss them!

In reality, there are more people who are unhappy than those who are happy. Students think that when a teacher teaches them everything they do not know, that teacher becomes the center of hope, the center of aspiration, and a leader who can take responsibility for their future. Students feel a desire to confess all their circumstances to their teacher and discuss them.

In the same way, if God exists, how wonderful it would be if He taught humanity from the position of the most caring and closest teacher, from the position of the closest parent. This is something anyone can think. However, this is not a simple issue.

What is the true path of life? In the world you are living in today, if you were to stop a passerby and ask, "Are you happy?" would there be anyone who would answer, "Of course, I am happy"? Certainly, some may answer that they are happy, but the majority would likely respond, "Well, I’m not sure." Some might even say, "What happiness? Where are the happy people?"

So, when you consider those responses, would there be more people answering that they are happy or more who say they are unhappy? Have you thought about it? Looking at you, I see many young students. When a teacher asks, should you not respond? Do you think more people would answer that they are happy or that they are unhappy? Even older adults and younger students would likely respond that they are unhappy.

Young kindergarteners may not have any complaints about their parents, so they might say they are happy. However, by the time they reach the fifth grade, they start to understand their family and society, and they develop their own standards of thought. If you ask boys and girls of that age, they will undoubtedly answer that they are unhappy. Moreover, all of you would likely answer, "We are unhappy." 

There are more people who say they are unhappy than those who say they are happy. If you were to go to someone who claims to be happy and investigate whether they truly live a happy life, you would find that this is not the case. They may be happy in their own lives, but when you look at their family, even if their parents are there and they have siblings, there may be disabled siblings or siblings who cannot study even if they want to. In this way, everyone has many shortcomings behind them. 

When you consider all of this, no matter how happy someone claims to be, when you look at the overall background or the family as a fence, you cannot say that the entire family is happy. 

Even looking at a single family, we feel that it is not a happy family but an unhappy one. Expanding this scope, the unhappy families that make up today’s society and nation are connected. In other words, countless unhappy families are now connected to South Korea. So, will a society or nation connected to these unhappy families be happy? Again, it is unhappy. The conditions for all actions.

Power comes from the mutual exchange between the subject and the object. However, even if there is a subject and an object, they do not exchange when there is a loss for either. Even if you cut off a neck, there is no exchange. For example, when a young man or woman in their adolescence is in love, both the man and the woman want to take each other as their object. In other words, they must meet in a way that is good for both. They will not give up their own unless they discover something that can be a plus for them. They do not want to give. If they find that living with that person will benefit them, meaning they will not incur a loss and will gain, they will want to exchange.

However, if from the very beginning, it is a minus, will they want to engage? They will absolutely not want to engage. Even when looking at the relationship between the subject and the object, until they find something from the other side that can be more plus than their own desired goal, they will not want to exchange. In other words, if a good outcome does not appear, they will not exchange.

What does it mean to be good? It means to be plus. What does it mean to be bad? It means that things are taken away, resulting in a loss and becoming minus. Good things are plus and prosper, while bad things are minus and perish. Therefore, even if there is a relationship between the subject and the object, if it can become minus, no matter how strong the force is applied, there will be no power of exchange. Power cannot arise. Is that right? Is it not?

From this perspective, the dialectic of communism is a logic that does not understand this. To acknowledge the confrontation of power, a relationship between the subject and the object must be established. This is the condition of goodness. When you conduct a chemistry experiment, you can see that elements do not act unconditionally. However, when elements have even a slight condition that can lead to a better and more plus outcome, they will act immediately. If even a little minus factor enters and infringes upon itself, it will absolutely not act. This universe has a self-protective function. This is a principle. It is a scientific principle. Do you understand?

Do you have a conscience action or not? The existence of conscience action means what? "Power." What does it mean that there is power? It means that a relationship between the subject and the object has already been established and is acting. It signifies that a subject and an object can progressively become plus for each other's purposes. When there is conscience action, should there be a subject of conscience or not? Should there be or not? "There should be." The existence of conscience action means that there is a subject and an object of conscience.

Humans are beings of results, not beings of motives. If they were beings of motives, it would mean that humans were born because they wanted to be born. Did you want to be born? Therefore, humans are beings of results.

Everything is based on the subject and the object. One eye alone cannot function. It is when the two eyes align with the eyebrows that one can see well. The ears also have two eardrums that resonate from the left and right. The same goes for the nose. Everything has a dual purpose. That is why the Unification Church has discovered the great principle of the action of unification.

In the relationship of the subject and object where power arises, if one side becomes minus, it will not act at all. In the relationship between the subject and the object, when both sides require a third purpose that can be plus, development occurs.

The law of love.

If an amoeba acts, there must be a relationship between the subject and the object. When a person with a subject and object relationship loves each other and exchanges physiological actions, life is born. An amoeba develops from itself. In development, plus and minus act from one. Thus, two purposes must become one result. Do you understand? This is the basis for development. When this is absent, there is no action. This is the principle.

When we look at the amoeba, can something larger than the amoeba come out from the action of giving and receiving? It must be larger to be considered developed, right? What this means is that if power has acted, greater power must emerge. In other words, it means that energy does not get consumed but rather generates greater energy. The principle of development is that the more energy acts, the more it must increase.

So what happens when it acts? It becomes smaller, right? When it acts, consumption occurs. Because of the absorption action, it must be supplied. Therefore, consumption occurs. The origin of life is the same. The question is whether power can arise from consumption. Does the output match the input? When you look at an electric motor, does the power of the electricity going in equal the power coming out? Does it get smaller or larger? "It gets smaller."

However, evolution implies that the output is larger. Can that happen? From the perspective of the principle of power, it is impossible. Therefore, this power must have a third force added. If that principle is correct, there would be a significant problem in this vast universe. That is why a third force is needed.

The Existence of God Seen Through the Mysterious Human Body
You want to give everything to parents who have loved you, right? You want to give even your body to someone you love, right? Also, when a person receives great grace, they want to give even their life. Isn’t that so? That is love.

200   The Mission of Unification Family
What we must first unify is Christianity. This is because numerous sects have divided and should not harbor animosities against one another; we must seek ways to unite regardless of the circumstances. This is not only what we humans desire, but it is also what God and Jesus wish for.

Yet, at the end of days, all of this must come to an end. When the end comes, the process of how humanity has lived on this earth will be revealed until their lives come to a close. Just as the trees reveal how they have lived throughout the year when the end of the autumn season arrives, the end of historical times will reveal the entirety of each religion. Not only religions but also humanity will be the same.

When looking at an individual, the existence of "me" is not just the individual you see today, whether it be Kim or Park. This is because we have inherited the bloodline and connections of our ancestors throughout historical times to reach the present. Thus, even when looking at one individual, the fruits they have inherited from their ancestors—whether they are good or bad—will inevitably be revealed at the end.

Just as it is with individuals, the same applies to families. Some families thrive while others do not, and this will be revealed at the end.

When a family is at the center, it influences the nation, and as many families are revealed, the current status of that family reflects the historical fate of the nation. If a family is like this, then the same goes for the nation. In the case of the Republic of Korea, despite the many twists and turns throughout its 5,000-year history, today’s Republic of Korea is a manifestation of historical fruits.

A good seed sown in good soil, nurtured by a good farmer, will grow into a bountiful harvest. However, if the ancestors did not establish a foundation capable of revival, that nation will inevitably become a developing country.

When viewed this way, as the end approaches, the processes a nation has gone through will gradually be revealed. Therefore, through the trials of rise and fall, at the end, every nation will not be the same. Countries that once boasted advanced civilizations in ancient times have now fallen into the status of developing or underdeveloped nations. We recognize this fact. In this regard, whether the end is good or bad, the historical outcomes will inevitably manifest according to the processes of history. The same applies to religions.

When observing human life, some live until 50 years, others until 70, 80, or even over 100 years. We learn through newspapers that people’s lifespans vary. Even when considering a person’s life, we see that each individual’s life ends at different ages. Thus, everything that begins must eventually come to an end.

The larger the religion, the more it shines in the end.
So, when we consider whether Christianity, Buddhism, Confucianism, or Islam will continue indefinitely, we find that religions that can inherit God’s providence and will will shine in the end. However, smaller religions that adapt to their environments will see their missions come to an end and will fade away.

Today, there are four major world religions. Among them, Christianity has the content that can influence the development of global civilization and determine human happiness and unhappiness. However, Christianity is also not exempt from this reality. It will not continue forever; there will come a time when it will end, just like the autumn season.

When the autumn season arrives, the lush leaves will begin to fall one by one, and Christianity will also face such a time. It is completely different from the spring season, where a single leaf grows into two, then four, and so on, becoming lush in summer. However, if a single stem is not strong, no matter how lush the leaves are, they will soon wither. During the summer, the stem may seem worthless, but it is precisely that stem that supports countless leaves. From that stem, new life and new value begin. Flowers bloom from the stem, and fruits are borne from it.

When looking at Christianity, there was the era of the early church, followed by a period of revival, and then a period of gradual development leading to a golden age. When the golden age arrives, it will inevitably lead to a saturation point, after which there will come a time of decline. This is similar to how all trees flourish in summer, but as autumn arrives, the leaves begin to fall, marking the beginning of a downward path. Thus, they fall from their peak. When they reach the bottom and rise again, they can sustain life.

When they rise again, those who possess the strength to maintain life can welcome a new spring. If they can sustain life, they can greet a new spring. However, if they lack the strength to maintain life, they will end with autumn and winter. By observing the four seasons of the year, we can understand this well.

When looking at a day, morning corresponds to spring, daytime to summer, evening to autumn, and night to winter. Similarly, life goes through youth, adulthood, and old age before death. The entire universe operates according to the law of cyclical movement: spring passes, summer comes; summer passes, autumn comes; autumn passes, winter comes. There is a time for beginnings, a time for flourishing, and then inevitably a time for bearing fruit. The time for bearing fruit is a time of reduction. It is when all the sap that has spread out is concentrated within a living organism to ripen the fruit. The leaves gradually wither, and the fruit absorbs sap from the tree, ripening over time.

Religions will also inevitably face a time akin to the autumn season. Every religion will encounter its autumn season. When the autumn season arrives, what happens? A new spring season can be welcomed through a religion that possesses the content to inherit a new era. Thus, a new religion can emerge, paving the way for a new era, a new spring, a new civilization, and a new cultural sphere. However, if this does not happen, it will come to an end.

Living centered on oneself
When you look at your daily life, whether you speak, act, or seek something, there is no one who lives centered on a third party rather than themselves. Speaking is centered on oneself, and acting is centered on oneself. Moreover, when considering the existence of "I," humans do not like to be treated poorly by others or to be in a passive position. We know that it is human nature to strive to connect our subjective content with the environment we are in as the subject.

Therefore, what we like ultimately is not what others like; it is only when we like something that it becomes truly enjoyable. Likewise, when we are sad, we are not sad because of others; we are sad centered on ourselves. When we say someone is a good person, it is only in recognition of our own existence that we say they are good.
It is not about saying that something is good centered around the position of the room. Also, when we say someone is a bad person, the center that can determine that badness is not the person we are dealing with, but rather, it is myself who becomes the center and decides that it is bad.

In this way, we know that we are moving to find the results that are established in relation to whom we are connected and who we have a relationship with. Regardless of the individual, when we ask what kind of person one should be, it is said that one should be a good person, and we hope to become that way. **The Standard for Going to Heaven**

Today, humanity must become the sons and daughters of God. But who has taken God's place? Satan has entered. Thus, humanity has become the sons and daughters of Satan. Therefore, to return to being God's children, we must cut off our ties with Satan and be grafted onto God.

That’s why Jesus came to this earth. Jesus said, “I am the way, the truth, and the life; no one comes to the Father except through me.” Jesus is the true olive tree. Fallen humanity must be grafted onto the true olive tree. To be grafted, all ties to the world must be severed. You must cut off your country, the world, your parents, and your spouse. If you want to go to heaven, you must do it that way.

Jesus came to this earth as a historical reality and told us to love Him more than anyone else—more than our mothers, fathers, spouses, or anyone else. He said that if we do not love Him more than anyone else, we cannot be His disciples. Why is that? If the love Jesus receives on this earth is less than the love under Satan's authority, can He be called the Son of God? If He receives a love that is worse than Satan's, He cannot be called the Son of God.

What is the standard for going to heaven? It is to love God more than your own children. Without loving God more, you cannot escape the realm of Satan. Therefore, if you do not love God more than your spouse, you cannot enter heaven. Fallen humanity has come out to the edge of the trap of love under Satan's authority, but has not completely escaped. Thus, you must not love your father or mother more than God.

Where does heaven begin? It begins with denying even the emotional origin from which you were born. Therefore, those who walk the path of virtue live a single life. However, there is a difficult problem here. In the future, the Lord of the Second Advent will come and easily resolve this issue, but until then, individuals will face problems.

Since there is no way forward focusing solely on personal salvation, humanity must save families. The Lord of the Second Advent comes to open the way for entire families to be saved. Today, Christians believe they will go to heaven by believing in Jesus, but they are all caught up in individualism. Originally, one does not go to heaven alone. If Adam and Eve had not fallen and remained in God's love, would they have gone to heaven or not? If that were the case, hell could not exist.

So, how does one go to heaven? It is a place where couples, centered on their marriage, lead their children. They go along with their sons and daughters and grandchildren, leading their lineage. Furthermore, it is a place where entire nations go. That is how the heavenly kingdom is formed. Heaven is established in this way. Today, people who believe in Christianity say they will go to heaven, but heaven is not a place you enter alone. You absolutely cannot go alone.

Why could Jesus not enter heaven? Heaven was created by God so that the unfallen living beings could enter. Humanity must be established according to these principled standards to enter heaven. Therefore, Jesus Himself must save fallen humanity and enter with His sons and daughters from the position of Adam and Eve, the parents of unfallen humanity. However, Jesus came alone; does He have descendants? Because He does not, He is in paradise. He is not able to enter heaven and is in a waiting room for heaven.

Thus, Jesus must come again to find a bride. Originally, Adam and Eve were to become a bride and groom in the Garden of Eden and go to heaven. Even though the ancestors of humanity fell, that principle remains, and Jesus must come to fulfill it. Because He went alone, He cannot enter heaven. He must come again and resolve matters on earth to go to heaven. Just as the Bible says, what is bound on earth must be loosed on earth.

**What is Satan?**

So, what did Satan do? How did Satan do it? Satan immobilized Adam and Eve with illicit love and made them his own. Originally, love is meant to be governed absolutely according to the principle of creation. Once a connection of love is made, it is governed eternally by blood ties. Because Satan violated this principle and robbed humanity's ancestors, God could not govern this love. God was meant to govern humanity based on love, but illicitly, Satan has bound humanity to himself based on this principle. Therefore, God must reclaim humanity from Satan. The struggle to find this lost child has been a problem for thousands of years.

So, what is Satan? What is Satan before God? God is a God of love. He is a being full of love. Why has God, who can forgive human mistakes thousands of times, never forgiven Satan even once? Why could He not show love to Satan?

Satan is what? He is a chief. Not a chief of some organization, but the enemy of love. The enemy of love, Satan, has slandered God. You must think about how much pain God has endured for 6,000 years under Satan's slander.

Since Satan cut off Adam and Eve, to restore this, we must cut off the very thing that was severed. Only then can restoration occur. Today, humans living on this earth, regardless of age or gender, are walking their life paths without knowing what kind of path it is, or they are trying to know while continuing on.
